(Second Sheet of the Shen Bao)

Current Commentary

The American Recovery Problem and Roosevelt's Monetary Policy By Ying

It has been more than half a year since the United States implemented the National Industrial Recovery Act. However, the ultimate goal of so-called restoring prosperity has yet to be realized. Low prices, overproduction, reduced trade, and increased unemployment—everything everywhere in the United States is plagued by the problem of economic depression, which remains very serious. Therefore, many people fundamentally doubt whether the strategies adopted by the Washington government can restore the past prosperity of capitalism. However, according to overseas news reports yesterday, the United States is now implementing a new policy. Compared with the previous strategies, such as suspending the gold standard and buying gold at home and abroad, it seems to have taken a further step. But from our observations, this new policy is still trapped in the snare of trying to raise prices through monetary policy.

The content of the new American policy has two important points: (1) All gold owned by the Federal Reserve Banks must be transferred to the U.S. Treasury Department, and the Treasury Department will provide the Reserve Banks with U.S. dollars of equal value as credit. (2) All cash must not circulate. Gold coins must be abolished and not redeemed. Private cash holdings must be turned over to the Treasury Department for purchase. In addition, there are three newly promulgated laws. The main significance lies in managing foreign exchange and prohibiting capital flight, which is also an inevitable step after prohibiting cash circulation within the country. The main points of the so-called new policy are as described above.

We must first understand what impact Roosevelt's new monetary policy has on the country. The basic purpose of the new monetary policy is to raise prices, especially to raise domestic prices in the United States. If prices can be raised to the level of 1926, then debts incurred at the same time in that year can be easily repaid from the debtor's point of view. Therefore, the U.S. authorities believe that if the cash value of the U.S. dollar can be reduced by 40%, the U.S. dollar value of commodities should also be raised by 40% accordingly. From this point of view, the value of commodities seems to be manipulated by the amount of gold content in the U.S. dollar. However, it is not known that the determining factor of commodity value lies in the actual purchasing power of society. Value can only increase when purchasing power is developed; otherwise, commodities will only be stockpiled forever, and how can value be raised? Leaving aside other considerations, just look at the American farmers, who are suffering because they have mountains of agricultural products rather than gold. The U.S. dollar value of gold can increase from $20.67 to $35, but the U.S. dollar value of agricultural products does not necessarily increase by the same amount, unless artificial methods are used to burn the agricultural products until the price is raised. From this point of view, the purpose of the new monetary policy, the so-called raising of prices, may not be possible to achieve.

The new American monetary policy may not have much impact on domestic prices, but it can be a way for the U.S. government to generate wealth and increase revenue more quickly and easily than any other method, such as raising taxes or borrowing money. According to U.S. President Roosevelt, the government will profit approximately 420 million yuan from the reduction in the pure gold content of the U.S. dollar, which is more than the entire year's revenue. This is the result of the transfer of gold management rights. However, what we must not forget is that the U.S. government has simultaneously suspended its obligation to pay government debts in pure gold. Therefore, in terms of impact, the only effect of Roosevelt's new policy still lies in this rather than elsewhere.

The Central Political Council Passed

Regulations for Mongolian Autonomy

Li Wenfan Appointed as National Government Committee Member

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council convened its 392nd meeting on the morning of the 17th. Attendees included Wang Zhaoming, Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Gu Mengyu, Kong Xiangxi, Dai Chuanxian, Zhang Qun, Zhu Jiahua, Shi Qingyang, Shi Ying, and over thirty others. Wang Zhaoming chaired the meeting, and the following resolutions were passed:

(A) The Regulations for Mongolian Autonomy are as follows: (1) Regarding the extent of autonomy in Inner Mongolia, the Category A measures proposed by the Mongolian representatives, which involve establishing autonomous regional governments in different districts, are deemed to be in line with the principles set by the Central Government and can be adopted. Separate measures will be drafted later regarding their regional affiliation, organizational authority, funding, and other aspects, and laws will be enacted and implemented. (2) Regarding the implementation procedures for Mongolian autonomy, it seems necessary to establish a preparatory office before the formal establishment of autonomous regional governments. However, the Central Government must send personnel to provide effective guidance, or the Central Government should appoint the chairman of the local provincial government as a special commissioner for guidance. The procedures for selecting personnel will be determined separately. (3) Regarding the scope of the Mongolian autonomous region, the establishment of the Mongolian autonomous region should be limited to areas without established county administrations. Two districts each will be established within the provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan. Their names will be the First Autonomous Region Government of the Republic of China (Mongolia), the Second Autonomous Region Government, and so on. However, if the two autonomous regions established within Chahar Province or Suiyuan Province are originally merged into one self-governing region, the respective provinces may report to the Ministry of Interior of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission for submission to the Executive Yuan for approval. Areas within the two provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan where county administrations have already been established, and which fall entirely under provincial administrative jurisdiction, or areas where regional complexities necessitate detailed demarcation, will be surveyed and demarcated by the provincial government in conjunction with the district government, and the results will be reported to the Ministry of Interior of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission for submission to the Executive Yuan for approval. The Alxa Ejin Banner region, originally under the jurisdiction of Ningxia Province, will not be included in the autonomous region. (4) Regarding the organization of the autonomous regional government: 1. The autonomous regional government will have five to fifteen members, with one serving as chairman and two as vice-chairmen, all of whom should be appointed by the Central Government and should be local residents in principle. 2. The district government will handle affairs through departments. 3. In order to discuss common matters among the autonomous regions, the Central Government will dispatch personnel to convene a joint meeting of the autonomous regions once a year. 4. The autonomous region will have a two-tiered district and banner system. Each district and banner will establish a people's self-governance organization, the details of which will be determined by law. 5. The location of the district government will be approved by the Central Government. (5) Regarding the subordination of the autonomous regional government, the Mongolian autonomous regional governments will be subordinate to the Executive Yuan and subject to the direction and supervision of the central departments in charge. (6) Regarding the authority of the autonomous regional government, the authority over national defense and military command within the Mongolian autonomous region, as well as matters related to foreign affairs, will be handled by the Central Government in a unified manner or delegated to the local provincial government for execution. Other matters deemed to have special characteristics by the Central Government may also be delegated to the local provincial government for handling. Mongolian and banner administration matters not delegated by the Central Government to the provincial government for handling will be handled by the district government in a unified manner. The district government may issue district orders and formulate specific rules within the scope of not conflicting with the laws and regulations of the Central Government and the local provincial government. However, measures that restrict the freedom of the people or increase the people's burden may not be implemented without the approval of the National Government. (7) Regarding the relationship between the provincial government and the autonomous regional government, various Mongolian and banner administration matters within the Mongolian autonomous region authorized by the Central Government to the provincial government will still be handled by the provincial government in a unified manner. Matters not authorized by the Central Government to the provincial government will be handled by the district government in accordance with the Central Government's directives. In cases involving the scope of provincial administration, consultations with the provincial government are still required. All Mongolian and banner administration matters and disputes between Mongolians and Han Chinese in areas where county administrations have already been established will still be handled by the local provincial government. When necessary, a special committee may be established to resolve disputes between the province and the district. The Central Government may entrust the provincial government to represent the Central Government in guiding the Mongolian district government in handling local autonomy. (8) Regarding the administrative expenses of the autonomous regional government, the administrative expenses of the autonomous regional government should be budgeted and approved by the Central Government for allocation and subsidy. All tax revenues should be divided into national taxes and local taxes in accordance with the standards set by the Central Government. All national taxes will be collected directly by the Central Government or delegated to the local provincial government for collection. All local taxes will be collected by the provincial government in areas where county administrations have already been established, and by the autonomous regional government in areas where county administrations have not yet been established. (9) Regarding the financial issues of the autonomous region, in areas that have been developed and where county administrations have already been established, all existing land rights of Mongolians and Han Chinese will remain unchanged. In Mongolian and banner areas that have not been developed and where county administrations have not been established, animal husbandry will be the main occupation, supplemented by agriculture. Citizens of the Republic of China, regardless of ethnicity, who have continuously resided in the region for more than one year, will have the right to engage in nomadic grazing and cultivation. If the district government deems it necessary to develop land within the autonomous region, it may report to the Central Government for approval at any time to open it freely for cultivation by Mongolians and Han Chinese. Livestock in undeveloped areas should be improved through various means, and the Central Government should establish cattle and sheep epidemic prevention stations and serum manufacturing branches in suitable locations to benefit animal husbandry and promote hygiene. Forests and minerals should be nationalized and developed by the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance should establish branches of the Central Bank in the various autonomous regions to serve as active financial institutions. (10) Regarding the education issues of the autonomous region, the issue of reforming the Mongolian education system and subsidizing Mongolian education expenses should be referred to the Ministry of Education in conjunction with the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission for overall planning and formulation of specific measures. (11) Regarding the judicial issues of the autonomous region, the matter should be referred to the Ministry of Justice in conjunction with the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission for formulation of specific measures.

B. The ordinance for the issuance of the Hubei Province Financial Consolidation Public Bonds of the Republic of China for 1934, totaling 4 million yuan, was approved in principle and sent to the Legislative Yuan.

C. The Central Executive Committee was requested to elect Li Wenfan as a member of the National Government Committee.

D. The allocation of 60,000 yuan in annual recurring expenses to subsidize schools in the late Premier's hometown was approved. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Nanjing) Zhao Taibao and fourteen other representatives of the Khalkha League and Banner of Inner Mongolia, regarding the Central Political Council's changes to the Mongolian autonomy regulations, went to the Central Political Council on the morning of the 17th to petition for the maintenance of the original plan and personally delivered a petition. The Political Council dispatched Secretary-General Tang Youren to receive them, who promised to convey the petition to the Central Political Council for adoption. The original petition stated: The eleven articles of the Mongolian autonomy regulations, negotiated by Minister Huang in Bailingmiao with the league and banner leaders and representatives, were repeatedly promised by Wang and Dai to be unchanged, which was deeply gratifying. However, it is now heard that as a result of repeated reviews by the council, due to the advocacy of one or two members, the original plan of two districts has been changed to four districts, with one league as one district, and areas where counties have been established and the three special banners of Alxa and Ejin have been excluded. Almost all of the original plan's spirit has been completely erased. The reason given is that the Suiyuan Provincial Government reported to the Central Government that the league leaders and deputy league leaders of the Ih Ju League had expressed their willingness to have one league as one autonomous region. This matter was entirely fabricated by the Suiyuan Provincial Government. In addition to a separate statement of the truth by the representatives of the Ih Ju League, it is noted that the original purpose of the leagues' request for autonomy was to unite against aggression. If the original one league is still used as one district, then what is the point of this extra effort? As for areas where counties have been established and the three banners of Alxa and Ejin, they are all part of the Mongolian territory. If they are not allowed to be included in the autonomous region, how will they be treated? Moreover, the original plan for Mongolian autonomy was negotiated by Minister Huang, who closely understood the actual situation of Mongolia, on behalf of the Central Government. If it is changed abruptly based on the advocacy of one or two individuals, it will not only damage the Central Government's prestige but also seem to be making fun of Mongolia. Now, Eastern Mongolia has fallen to Japanese traitors, and no measures for relief from the Central Government have been heard. For Western Mongolia, which has no guarantee for the morning, it is not willing to give them the opportunity to save themselves and the country. The Suiyuan Provincial Government has repeatedly sent personnel to various leagues to use coercion and bribery to make them express opposition to Mongolian autonomy, causing League Leader Yun of the Ulanqab League to resign against his will, and the Shiliingol League did not send representatives to Beijing. How could Inner Mongolia, which has supported the Central Government for more than a decade as one day, have reached this point? Now, the rumor that the puppet organization has been changed to the Manchu-Mongol Empire and that Puyi will restore the throne and move the capital to Chengde is becoming more and more real. If this rumor comes true, then not only will a major change occur between Mongolia and the Central Government, but Mongolia itself will be doomed. At that time, what methods will the Central Government have to deal with the aftermath, apart from empty words of long-term resistance? What methods will the Suiyuan Provincial Government have to salvage the situation, apart from perishing together? We, the Mongolians who will inevitably perish without developing resistance, cannot but hold endless regret for the Central Government and the Suiyuan Provincial Government. Esteemed members of the council, with your profound and far-reaching plans for the country, you must be aware of the aforementioned difficult situation. We earnestly request that you maintain the original plan of the eleven articles of the Mongolian autonomy regulations negotiated by Minister Huang so that Mongolian autonomy can be realized as soon as possible. We will be grateful for your great virtue beyond measure. If you do not heed our plea and still pass the reviewed plan, then our leagues and banners will absolutely not dare to accept it. The representatives can only return to Mongolia in tears and await our fate. (Special dispatch, 17th)

Panchen Arrives in Guihua

Guihua The Panchen Lama, with his entourage of over sixty people in fifteen cars, departed from Bailingmiao at 6 a.m. on the 16th, rested briefly at Zhaohuo, and arrived in Suiyuan in the evening. Fu Zuoyi, Leng Rong, Pan Wang, and others greeted him outside the Beishaliang Pass. Lama musicians, military bands, and military police were all lined up to welcome him. Crowds lined the streets, creating an unprecedentedly enthusiastic atmosphere. Soldiers from Fu's troops were stationed along the route to maintain order. The residence was set up at the Suiyuan Hotel. It was reported that a banquet was held in the evening to welcome the Panchen Lama, with Leng Rong and dignitaries from all walks of life invited to accompany him. The Panchen Lama, suffering from a cough and toothache, sent his Secretary-General Liu Jiaju to meet with reporters. Liu said that the Panchen Lama was summoned to Beijing by Premier Wang and others to attend the Fourth Plenary Session and discuss border affairs. He originally planned to go to Ih Ju League to chant scriptures before going to Beijing, but upon hearing the news of the Dalai Lama's death, he canceled his trip to Ih Ju League and sent Ma Shu Kanbu with eleven lamas to represent him at Ih Ju League to chant scriptures. The Panchen Lama was extremely saddened by the Dalai Lama's death and had been unable to eat or sleep for several days. In addition to issuing a notice to lamas in monasteries throughout Mongolia, Qinghai, and Tibet to chant scriptures in remembrance and expressing condolences at all offices, he also recited sutras himself to help the Dalai Lama transcend. Regarding the political and religious affairs of Tibet after the Dalai Lama's death, the Panchen Lama earnestly hopes that the Central Government will first send personnel to Tibet to inspect the situation. The Panchen Lama will return to Ih Ju League and then Qinghai after consulting with Premier Wang and others in Beijing to prepare for his return to Tibet. The Panchen Lama plans to stay in Suiyuan for one day and leave Suiyuan on the 18th, stopping briefly at Ping to proceed to Beijing to attend the Plenary Session. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Beiping) The Panchen Lama is scheduled to depart from Suiyuan for Ping on the 18th. Mongolian paper money is worth only a few cents per yuan. Grain prices in the Northwest are low, harming farmers, and rural areas are bankrupt. (Special dispatch, 17th)

Recently Returned to Lhasa

Soviet Russia Constructs

Giant Aircraft

Carrying a Load of Six or Seven Tons, Accommodating Over Sixty People

Complete Communication Equipment

Specifically for Propaganda Purposes

(London) Details regarding the giant aircraft currently being manufactured by Soviet Russia were disclosed today by the information office of the Soviet Embassy to reporters from the Standard Evening News. According to reports, this giant aircraft will be used specifically for propaganda purposes after its construction. The aircraft will be equipped with a printing press, a telephone, a movie projector, wireless radio, and wireless movies, among other things. In addition to the flight crew, the aircraft will also carry many typists, telephone operators, and movie drivers. The total load will be approximately six or seven tons. Whenever the aircraft arrives at a city, it will fly at a very low altitude, and at the same time, use a large sound amplifier to broadcast pre-arranged programs to the entire city. Leaflets and pamphlets pre-printed in the aircraft can also be distributed at the same time. The aircraft can also emit smoke in the sky to form letters, which can be seen from two miles away. The entire crew of the aircraft will be approximately sixty-five people. However, British experts are skeptical of this claim but are willing to observe its progress. (National Electric, 16th)

Saar Issue

Situation Extremely Serious

Governing Commission Submits Report

League of Nations to Discuss Issue at End of Week

(Geneva) The situation regarding the Saar issue is now more serious than expected. There is currently a strong rumor that the League of Nations Administrative Council will discuss the occupation of the Saar by international troops at the end of this week. As for whether the Saar plebiscite in 1935 will be postponed, the Administrative Council will make a decision. If it decides to postpone the plebiscite, Germany will definitely take special actions because Hitler wants to rescue the territory without waiting for the self-determination vote, that is, to assign the territory to Germany. Because once the self-determination vote is held, the outcome will be irreversible, many people advocate postponement to wait for the situation in Germany to change and allow the Saar people to become true Germans. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

Pongou Attends Senate

Explains Foreign Policy

Ensuring Austrian Independence and Maintaining European Balance

Does Not Want to Encircle Germany, Seeks Cooperation

(Paris) The Senate discussed foreign policy questions. Foreign Minister Pongou stood up to answer and explained the various current foreign issues. First, he said that although France does not make a fuss about international issues, it has already expressed its opinions when necessary. There is no reason to be impatient or anxious about the current situation.

Saar Plebiscite

As for the Saar issue, France has already expressed its views. Only the local people have the right to decide whether to hold a plebiscite, which France cannot abandon. What France can do is, as a member of the League of Nations, participate in the matter in Geneva. The only thing France cares about is ensuring that the people there can freely express their opinions and not be treated unfairly because of their expressions in the future.

Maintaining Austrian Independence

As for Austria, which is being oppressed by the Hitler Party, and atrocities occur from time to time, Austrian independence is actually the key to the European balance of power and must be maintained. France and Italy share the same opinion on this matter. Although the above-mentioned matters concern major principles, they are ultimately passive policies.

No Intention of Encirclement Germany

Apart from this, France must continue to strive for construction in diplomacy without any interruption. When the political evolution of the new Germany causes anxiety, France wants to unite all countries that feel the same anxiety so that all countries determined to maintain peace can unite and strengthen their forces based on international cooperation. There is no intention of encircling Germany. If Germany wants to join these countries, the right is in Germany's own hands. Germany previously suggested signing a non-aggression treaty, which France has already accepted. What its true intentions are can be seen from this.

Maintaining Old Friendship with Satellites

Pongou continued that France still maintains old friendship with its allied countries and does not relax in the slightest. It has become closer to Italy due to the signing of the Four-Power Pact, but France does not alienate its allied countries because of this. This can be seen from various published documents and exchanges of notes. The understanding between France and its allied countries is more vibrant and active than before. France sees this understanding not as one group opposing other groups, but as part of an overall plan to build peace within the scope of the League of Nations.

European Security Net

France intends to expand the scope of this consultation and turn it into a European security net. Although this security net is not yet fully organized, it has made great progress in recent months. France maintains the original treaties between itself and Poland and the countries of the Little Entente. At the same time, it provides diplomatic assistance to these countries to improve their relations with Italy, Soviet Russia, the Balkan countries, and Turkey.

Improved Franco-Italian Relations

Pongou continued that the relations between France and Italy have completely changed, and it is a definite fact that the relations between the countries of the Little Entente and Italy are improving. The transformation of the countries of Central Europe requires the participation of Italy and the countries of the Little Entente. If relations improve with each other, then this participation is possible.

Successful Soviet Policy

France implements a Soviet policy in the eastern border of Europe. Although Soviet Russia is engaged in revolutionary construction internally, it is actually a conservative force for the current order in Europe in terms of international relations. Because France cannot have a comprehensive security plan internationally at present, it is gradually signing various partial treaties for relief. This kind of partial treaty increases day by day, and it will be able to accumulate into a fur coat from many small pieces and become a peaceful construction.

Striving for Peace Building

Although the entire plan for peaceful construction is difficult to establish suddenly, it has been partially realized. Soviet Russia has signed non-aggression treaties with many countries, and its actions are the same as France's. Although Soviet Russia is not within the League of Nations, it provides assistance to the member states, and the member states also assist it. The form of the treaties signed by Soviet Russia with various countries is not as precise as the Locarno Treaty, but its function is also equal. Although the Locarno Treaty has been criticized by all parties, the promises it contains do have the value of the old alliance treaties. Since the treaties signed by Soviet Russia with various countries have the same function as the Locarno Treaty, then their value is worthy of our praise.

On the Balkan Question

Peng Gu Xuan discussed the Balkan question, saying that Yugoslavia, Romania, Greece, and Turkey would soon sign a non-aggression treaty to guarantee the territorial integrity of each signatory, and he hoped that Bulgaria could also participate. Italy has no objection to this matter.

Consistently Supporting the League of Nations

Finally, Peng Gu said that France will always express complete trust in the League of Nations, and its attitude need not be repeated.

Parliamentarians Speak One After Another, All Distrusting Germany

After Peng Gu finished speaking, parliamentarian Goterot spoke, vigorously explaining the insecurity of Franco-German compromise, and also specifically raised reservations about Franco-Russian consultation, saying that in the event of war, one cannot rely on Russian military assistance, and demanded guarantees for the implementation of the Franco-Russian agreement. Subsequently, former President Miller Hangwei delivered a speech, urging the French people to unite sincerely and expressing distrust of Germany's peace proposals. After Mr. Miller finished speaking, former Ambassador to Rome, Ju Fenal, delivered a speech, saying that France should not always listen to others in international negotiations, especially in Franco-German negotiations. Ju Fenal believed that there was an opportunity to maintain peace in Franco-German negotiations, and also said that France's alliances with various countries must be placed in the entire construction of Europe to be effective. Finally, he spoke broadly about the impropriety of infringing on the territorial integrity and sovereignty of other countries, believing that there is already a possibility of separate unity among nations, but the scope of unity must not be too broad, and its largest scope belongs to the League of Nations, etc. At this point, the meeting was adjourned and scheduled to reconvene on Thursday. (Havas News Agency, 16th)

Severe Earthquake in India

Thousands Dead and Injured, Over Ten Thousand Houses Destroyed

Prosperous Cities Turned into Rubble Fields

Bihar Province Suffers the Most

Bombay - An earthquake occurred in India on Sunday, causing significant damage. The earthquake area is in the Ganges River basin, with Muzaffarpur and Patna being the worst affected. All streets in Muzaffarpur have collapsed, and corpses and rubble are scattered all over the streets. The estimated number of deaths is in the thousands. Railway and telegraph communications are completely disrupted. After planes flew to the disaster area for inspection and returned here, aviators claimed that the once prosperous cities are now only rubble piles, and they are also flooded by large amounts of water, making the scenery in the disaster area even more desolate. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

Calcutta - According to reports received from various areas affected by yesterday's earthquake, the total number of casualties will be greater than estimated. The latest survey reports 100 deaths, 500 injuries, many of them seriously injured, 12,000 houses destroyed, and property losses amounting to £750,000. It is now known that the epicenter of the earthquake is in the Ganges River region and the foothills of the Himalayas. The worst-hit area is Patna and its surrounding areas in Bihar Province, with a total of 56 deaths and 407 injuries. Due to the severity of the disaster, it was temporarily announced that there would be a two-day holiday, during which all transactions were suspended. In Bihar Province, six people were killed in Bagpur. Mrs. Bai Lang, the wife of the manager of the Jamalpur Railway Engineering, did not die, but her children were killed. They were crushed to death when their houses collapsed. Sixteen people died in the Jamalpur market, and 500 houses were destroyed. When the earthquake occurred, the city center was extremely chaotic, and even the railway staff dormitories were uninhabitable. Telegraph and telephone lines in some locations were destroyed. The Indian government has sent two planes to investigate the disaster situation in Muzaffarpur. Several railways and new bridges in Gorakhpur were destroyed and are currently under repair. (Reuters News Agency, 16th)

English Times Newspaper Commentary

The Issue of the Pseudo-Manchu Usurpation

(London) This morning, The Times published a lengthy editorial commenting on the issue of the restoration of the Qing Dynasty in Manchuria. It first explained the reason for Japan's support of the imperial system, stating: "European and American countries regard 'Manchukuo' as a puppet in the hands of the Japanese, or as a Japanese colony. Japanese politicians believe that after the declaration of the imperial system, the status of the new organization of Manchuria will be elevated and have a more lasting appearance. Japanese politicians also believe that two results can be obtained after Manchuria declares an imperial system. Firstly, the world is deeply afraid that Japan will eventually annex Manchuria. Now that Manchuria has declared an imperial system, this fear can be eliminated. Secondly, a part of Japanese public opinion supports the annexation of Manchuria and is quite inflammatory. Now that the imperial system has been declared, this kind of incitement can also be stopped." The Times then stated its own opinion, saying that although Japan admits it does not want to make Manchuria a colony, it may satisfy some people, but whether the current relationship between Japan and "Manchukuo" will not change after the political system of Manchuria changes, European and American public opinion does not dare to lightly believe and still awaits further proof. On the Chinese side, the restoration of Manchuria is enough to worry the majority of Republicans, because Manchuria is close to the old capital of China and is indeed a threat at the flanks. Moreover, the restoration of Manchuria is tantamount to refusing to recognize China's sovereignty over Manchuria again. This will not only fail to improve relations between China and Japan but also increase the difficulties for those who intend to find a temporary solution between China and Japan and "Manchukuo." (Havas dispatch, 17th)

Intermodal Packages

In order to prevent illegal traitors from using intermodal packages to transport drugs, it has ordered all intermodal routes to strictly inspect the intermodal packages received at the originating and destination stations from the date of the order, and to investigate the nature of the packages and the shipping situation, and to take thorough precautions to cut off the source of drugs. If drugs are found in any route in the future and it is proved that they were indeed transported by the protected road, the personnel in charge of the originating and destination stations will be severely investigated. Japanese and Puppet Troops in the War Zone

Organize Special Service Agencies

Specializing in Investigating Anti-Japanese Activities and Connecting with Puppet Troops

A Beiping dispatch states that since the signing of the ceasefire agreement between China and Japan, the war zone should have been returned to our country by the Japanese side long ago. However, Yuguan and various passes on the Great Wall have been negotiated repeatedly by the North China authorities and the Japanese side since last winter until now, but there has been no result. During this time, the Japanese and puppet troops have intensified their activities in various counties within the war zone along the Great Wall passes. According to a secret investigation by a certain party, from December 26th of last year to the beginning of this month, puppet troops in seven places in Tangshan, Linyu, Luanxian, Funing, Qian'an, Zunhua, and Sanhe dispatched troops to set up agencies and carry out various activities. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

▲Tangshan (1) The Japanese Army Garrison Headquarters in Tangshan plans to organize a special service agency specializing in investigating anti-Japanese activities and contacting puppet troops. It can be established after Yang Yuling returns to Tangshan. Yang Yuling once served as the liaison section chief of Li Jichun's troops. (2) Li Jichun, Liu Zuozhou, Zhao Lei, and others have news of going to Tangshan to organize a liaison office. (3) The Japanese Military Police Sub-Station in Tangshan City currently employs many Chinese people specializing in investigating anti-Japanese activities. (4) There is a long-distance bus operated by the Japanese in Tangshan City, traveling between Fengrun and Yutian. (5) The War Zone Security Team frequently goes to Shenyang, with unknown missions. (6) There are more than 300 old troops of Li Jichun stationed in Xiaoji Town, more than 30 miles southeast of Tangshan, with more than 100 rifles, led by Ma Hanzhang and Sha Dabao. (7) Gambling is rampant in Tangshan City. More than 100 gamblers were arrested last time. Recently, openly gambling places in Beishan have gradually increased again. (8) There are about 200 Japanese and Korean stores in Tangshan City, most of which gamble and sell drugs.

▲Linyu (1) The Jiukoumen is stationed with a part (one squadron) of the 14th Brigade, equipped with communication equipment and military vehicles. From north of Yuguan, pedestrians are prohibited from passing through, seemingly becoming a fortress area. (2) More than 600 newly arrived puppet troops were stationed in Dongluo City on December 27th. (3) Recently, rumors have been rampant in Yuguan, and residents have been moving away.

▲Luanxian (1) There are about 150 officers and soldiers in the Luanxian Garrison, with more than 130 rifles and six machine guns, stationed in Daonan and Daobei. There is a radio station in the South Camp. The commander is Captain Shimizu. (2) The Kwantung Army Logistics Sub-Station is located in Luanxian, responsible for transporting matters from Xifengkou to Rehe by Matsuda Kikuma. Now that the Wanhe River is frozen, Matsuda has returned to Yuguan. (3) Luanxian has a Japanese police and military police dispatch station. (4) The transportation of the Luan River is managed by the Luan River Transportation Management Office, which is directly under the Kwantung Army Branch Supervisory Department. (5) Japanese troops frequently travel to and from the Luan River Railway Bridge.

▲Funing (1) A part of the 14th Brigade of the Kwantung Army is stationed at Jielingkou, about a small group. (2) The Japanese troops in Taitouying have all withdrawn to Jianchangying, claiming that the area is a buffer zone when they withdrew. (3) According to a report from Qiangou Town on December 26th, there are about 1,000 bandits such as [Black Dragon], [Little Pug], and [Jinshuidian] occupying the area.

▲Qian'an No Japanese or puppet troops are stationed at Lengkou and its nearby passes. However, the Japanese troops in Jianchangying strictly check pedestrians at Lengkou and its nearby passes, and boundary markers are built at each pass, with the words [Manchukuo Border North from Here] and [Wangdao Paradise] and other slogans.

▲Zunhua (1) On January 6th, Hirazawa Kiichi, the new captain of the 30th Regiment of the Sazhi Brigade stationed in Malanyu, led more than 20 soldiers and two companies of puppet troops to Shimen Town, claiming to be there to prevent Liu Guitang. (2) After the puppet troops stationed in Malanyu were taken over by the Second Battalion (Song Dingming) of the Second Regiment of the Rehe Garrison Army (Brigade Commander Zhang Junzhe, son of Zhang HaiPeng), the original Third Battalion of the regiment, which was stationed there, was still stationed in Zunhua and returned to Jianchangying on the 28th.

▲Sanhe (1) Chiba Noriyoshi, the special service battalion commander of the 11th Squadron of the Sazhi Brigade, and Tozawa Irusan Hideo, led 40 soldiers, one cart, and three Chinese, arrived in Sanhe at 5 p.m. on the 5th from Malanyu via Jixian, stationed in the Silimen area, and hired locals to lead them to Zhanggezhuang, Yutian, Pinggu, and other areas to scout the terrain. (3) According to a telephone report on January 11, the aforementioned Japanese troops had all withdrawn to Malanyu at 7 a.m. today and were scheduled to camp at Ma Zhongqiao that night. (16th)

Guangdong Troops are Assembled and Enter Fujian

Under the Command of Huang Renhuan

The Huang and Li Divisions are the Main Force

A Shantou dispatch reports that after the Central Army occupied Yanping Shuikou, drastic changes occurred inside Fujian Province. The troops of Zhang Yan, Qu Shounian, and others in southern Fujian have all entered the coastal area of ​​Putian and Xianyou. The garrison in Zhangzhou and Longyan is empty. Xiamen has been garrisoned by the navy. The 19th Route Army only maintains the line from Zhangzhou to Tong'an, Jiangdong Bridge, and along the railway to Shima. The four counties of Dongshan, Zhao'an, Yunxiao, and Zhangpu have also been recovered by the old troops of Zhang Zhen using the strength of the militia. The county magistrate of Zhao'an, Yang Bokhan, the county magistrate of Yunxiao, Hu Pinsan, and the county magistrates of Dongshan and Zhangpu have all fled to Xiamen. The counties in southern Fujian have recently fallen into a state of anarchy. Local militiamen have risen up one after another, all claiming to be the Fujian Anti-Rebel Army of Southern Fujian, designated by the Central Government, with the name of a certain detachment or company. Zhang Bingzhen, who calls himself the Second Detachment, united Wu Shan's Shen Donghai troops in Erdu, Zhao'an County, and launched an offensive with considerable momentum. The people are extremely uneasy. Many Fujianese have moved to Huanggang and Chaoshan in Guangdong Province. Zhang Ruigui's division, Zhong Fangjun's regiment, is stationed in Raoping County, guarding the Fenshui Pass. The pass is on the mountain, and the terrain is very majestic. Since last month, Zhong's troops have been digging trenches and building fortifications at the pass, and sentries have been placed in Zhao'an territory, only seven or eight miles away from the county seat, to protect the land transportation between Fujian and Guangdong. Recently, the local area in southern Fujian has been chaotic. The Central Government telegraphed Guangdong to send troops into Fujian to maintain local order. Cai Tingkai also telegraphed Guangdong, requesting Guangdong troops to enter western Fujian to suppress the communist bandits, because the original Xie Dingxin regiment of the 19th Route Army was in the Longyan area, and the regiment has now been transferred elsewhere. The Fujian side hopes that the Guangdong troops will enter the area to prevent the bandits in Changting and Liancheng from taking the opportunity to invade. Due to the needs of the times and the urging of both sides, the Chaoshan Guangdong troops have decided to enter Fujian under the command of Huang Renhuan. The greatest purpose is nothing more than to prevent and suppress communist bandits and maintain local order. As for the deployment situation, Zhang Ruigui, the division commander stationed in Chaozhou, has been holding meetings at the division headquarters for days. On the 10th, he inspected the trenches on the Phoenix Mountain at the junction of Chao'an and Raoping, and inspected the troops stationed at Hukou Mountain in Huanggang along the Chaoqian Road to Qiandong. On the 12th, he went to the Huanggang regiment headquarters and inspected Fenshui Pass, and additionally transferred a regiment to Raoping County, which can enter Fujian at any time. In addition, Huang Renhuan's division, which was originally stationed in Shanghang, Wuping, and Jiaoling, has also been ordered to move. Li Zhenliang's division stationed in Xingning and Wuhua has moved to Dapu and entered Yongding. It is heard that the Huang and Li divisions are the main force entering Fujian. The two regiments of the Li Division that were originally stationed in Lianhe and Ping have now been transferred to Xingning. The upper reaches of the Dongjiang River are all stationed by Chen Zhang's brigade, in joint defense with Longguang's division in Huiyang. The Guangdong troops entering the Fujian army are currently being deployed. It is said that Huang Renhuan is responsible for commanding the troops, and Li Yangjing is responsible for the military affairs of the Fujian-Jiangxi border bandits. Zhang Ruigui is still responsible for the Chaoshan coast. Recently, many machine guns, mortars, and bullets have been shipped from Guangzhou and distributed to the troops entering Fujian for replenishment. The warehouse at the Meixian airport has been completed, and all the aircraft of the Fifth Squadron have gathered in Meixian, flying over western Fujian and southern Jiangxi every day to investigate. The Guangzhou Air Force has transferred another Second Squadron to Shantou for long-term stationing, specializing in reconnaissance in southern Fujian. The troop movements have been extremely busy in recent days. The postal and telegraph offices have added many inspectors. Military movements and the comings and goings of officers are absolutely not allowed to be sent. Private letters involving the political situation or discussing current affairs are given special attention by the inspectors. (12th)

Lu Army

Night Assault on Bandit Liu

Bandit Liu Briefly Raided Shandong Province

Refugees from Southern Hebei Fled to Linqing

Jinan Correspondence: Liu Guitang's bandit gang, originally a group of so-called "Green Forest heroes" in southern Shandong, has transitioned between banditry and military service countless times. This time, starting from Chicheng in the south, they are harassing the border between Hebei and Shandong, aiming to return to their old nest at Baodugang in southern Shandong, or to go to Henan to join the bandit gang of Cui Bangjie. Xia Ziming's brigade, formerly under Liu, has surrendered to the government but did not accompany Liu. However, according to reports, Liu is still leading no fewer than three to four thousand men, with mortars, machine guns, cavalry, and infantry, still resembling an army. The places they have passed through in recent days have mostly been completely looted. Localities that welcome and entertain them are only chosen for wealthy ransom demands. Once Liu leaves, resistance or interception leads to widespread looting and brutal village massacres. They disarm local militias and police, and incorporate bandits and vagrants into their ranks. As of today (the 15th), reports indicate that Bandit Liu is still in southern Hebei. If they don't flee back to Shandong, they will certainly enter Henan. The troops of the three provinces have been mobilized to encircle and suppress them. On the Shandong side, there are the 74th Division under Li Hanzhang, the 81st Division under Zhan Shutang, the 2nd Route Militia under Zhao Renquan, the Cavalry Regiment under Li Xuande, and the Provincial Border United Village Association, all cooperating in blocking and suppressing. Bandit Liu has been observing for several days but has not dared to enter Shandong rashly. However, small groups of three or five bandits occasionally slip through to cause harm, but these have been quickly dealt with. According to a telephone report from Linqing at 9:00 PM tonight (the 15th), the main force of Bandit Liu was lingering in the Laoguanzhai area of Weixian County in southern Hebei this morning (the 15th). That location is only eighty li from Linqing, forty li from Xiabusi, a subordinate town of Linqing, seventy li from Qiulin in Shandong, and forty-five li from Matou Town in Qiuxian County. After receiving the report, Zhao Renquan, the Deputy Commander of the Northern Shandong Garrison and Commander of the 2nd Route Militia, immediately led his directly controlled Mixed Regiment and Li Xuande's Cavalry Regiment out of Shandong Province, advancing towards Weixian to intercept and suppress Bandit Liu. Upon hearing the news, Bandit Liu immediately fled southwest from Weixian, and around noon, they actually occupied Matou Town in Qiuxian County, Shandong. Zhao led his troops in hot pursuit, and by evening, Liu's forces had retreated from Shandong Province (Matou Town is only twenty-five li from Qiuxian City) and fled to Quzhou County in Hebei Province (forty-five li from Qiuxian County), occupying the Longtang Town area. They stayed there that night, and Zhao continued to lead his troops in relentless pursuit. That evening, the 2nd Route Militia and Li Xuande's Cavalry Regiment advanced to Zhen Dongbao and were in the midst of a night assault. Longtang Town, occupied by Bandit Liu, is forty li from Quzhou and northeast of Quzhou City. According to a telephone call from Liaocheng, Sun Tonggang and Wang Zuwen flew over western Shandong in Airplane No. 2 today to scout out bandit activity. They saw over a thousand of Bandit Liu's men north of Qiuxian City, appearing to be fleeing back to southern Hebei, and have reported this to the provincial authorities.

It is also reported that Li Hanzhang, the Commander of the 74th Division and Commander of the Northern Shandong Garrison, arrived in Linqing this afternoon (the 15th) from Dezhou to command the various troops and militias in suppressing Bandit Liu. People from Weixian County and Quzhou County in southern Hebei are fleeing to Linqing to seek refuge, bringing the old and the young in an endless stream. Their descriptions of Bandit Liu's devastation are extremely tragic, with massacres and looting leaving nine out of ten homes empty, causing great sorrow (15th).

Great Victory in Suppressing Bandits in Southern Hubei

丨Refugees from Eastern Hubei Resettle and Cultivate Land in Northern Hubei丨

Hankou Correspondence: After suffering setbacks in Puqi and Chongyang, the remaining bandits in southern Hubei, led by Zhang Shou, the self-proclaimed Third Division Commander, and Ye Jinbo, the Deputy Commander of the Jiangxi-Hubei Division, fled to the Mushigang, Zhengjunyou, and Yaji Mountain areas of Yangxin County. Chen Jicheng commanded the 26th Division under Guo Rudong, the New 7th Brigade under Li Zongjian, and the 33rd Brigade under Liu Peixu to jointly encircle and suppress them, and the bandits were defeated again. Chen sent a telegram to Hankou on the 15th reporting the victory, stating briefly: "The bandits' Third Division and Jiangxi-Hubei Division, numbering about four to five thousand men with over three thousand guns, began crossing the river at Qiaopu on the 11th. They were intercepted by our troops and pursued to Zouma Li, Wangwen, and Zijing Mountain. Our troops encircled and suppressed them on all sides, engaging in fierce combat throughout the day, with bayonet charges, routing the bandits. In this battle, Li Zongjian's New 7th Brigade captured over 270 rifles, over 20 pistols, and 1 machine gun, and captured alive the bandits' Third Division Chief of Staff, one Regimental Commander, and one Operations Section Chief. Guo Rudong's 26th Division and Liu Peixu's 37th Brigade also captured hundreds of guns, banners, and a large amount of baggage. In total, four to five hundred guns were captured, and three to four hundred men were captured alive. This battle is the first major victory in bandit suppression in southern Hubei in recent years," and so on.

The remaining bandits in eastern Hubei have now been completely annihilated, and the number of civilians moving out of the bandit areas is increasing daily. They will all be moved to northern Hubei, where they will be given land to cultivate. According to investigations, there are over 400,000 mu of public wasteland in northern Hubei. In northern Xiangyang alone, there are over 300,000 mu, and in the southeastern part, there are 70,000 mu. Giving each person ten mu of land would be more than enough to accommodate the existing 20,000-plus people. In addition, there are 700 mu of wasteland in Wuchang in southern Hubei, 7,700 mu in Jiayu, 1,300 mu in Jianli in western Hubei, 40 mu in Qishui in eastern Hubei, 140 mu in Yingcheng in central Hubei, and 500 mu in Anlu, Yunmeng, and Baokang in northern Hubei, which could accommodate over 10,000 more refugees (16th).

Songjiang

The Chen Family in Tanpailou Was Robbed

Four bandits with painted faces broke into the Chen Xueqi family home in Tanpailou of this city on the night of the 16th, digging a hole in the wall and entering the inner room. The owner, Chen Xueqi, woke up upon hearing the noise, but was unable to resist the bandits. They broke into the inner room and stole two gold rings and fifty silver dollars before fleeing with a whoop. By the time the winter defense police were notified, it was too late to track them down.

Suzhou

Murderer Executed by Hanging

Liu Gensan from Yixing knew Xu Shuangxi from the same village. Due to lending relationships, there was some animosity. Xu had a neighbor, Wang Laowu, who made a living selling red pills. Because Xu often made false claims, on June 3rd of the 21st year [of the Republic], he bribed Liu to Xu's home, using the excuse of going to listen to storytelling outside Zhongshan Gate together, inviting Xu out. Together with two unnamed red pill peddlers from Changzhou, they dragged Xu to the back of the Tianhou Temple, hacked him to death with a knife, and placed the body in an old coffin in the Yizhong cemetery, hoping to cover up their traces. Later, village chief Tan Hongzhang discovered it and reported it to the district, who arrested Liu and brought him to the county government for interrogation. He was sentenced to death. Liu refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. After three trials, the appeals were rejected. Yesterday (the 17th) at 8:00 AM, the High Court sent prosecutor Zhan Dufen to supervise the police in executing Liu by hanging at the Third Sub-prison execution ground.

Sailing Boat Robbed in Broad Daylight

Yesterday (the 16th) at 10:00 AM, a sailing boat traveling from Xishan to Suzhou was passing the Yushan area by the lake when it was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with ten male bandits and one female bandit on board. They were disguised and armed, and they moved the cargo on the boat to their boat, causing a loss of several hundred dollars.

Wuxi

Fire in Dazhi Alley

There are thirteen households in Dazhi Alley near the suspension bridge outside the west gate of this county. The night before (the 16th) at around 8:00 PM, Wu Afu, who sells beef, returned home to sleep. He accidentally knocked over the kerosene lamp on the table, causing it to ignite the bedding. It was impossible to put out the fire, and it quickly spread. The fire broke through the roof and the flames lit up the sky, spreading to the neighboring homes of Xi Jinbao, Wang A’quan, Wu Jida, Wu A’pang, Wu A’ting, Xi Rulin, Wu A’zhao, Wu A’kun, Zhang Fushou, and Wang A’san. When the fire brigades from various sections heard the alarm, they arrived at the scene to put out the fire. Because the fire was so intense, firefighters Wang Jingen and Mao Shanggen fell into the fire pit one after another. Fortunately, they were rescued, but they were seriously injured. Mao Shanggen's life is in danger and he is currently being treated at Puren Hospital. In total, eleven houses were burned down, resulting in significant losses.

Problems Arise During Chamber of Commerce Re-election

The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce recently held its re-election. Eight executive committee members were elected: Qian Sunqing, Wu Shimei, Cheng Jingdong, Jiang Huanqing, Li Zhongchen, Chen Zhanru, Wu Xiangqing, and Zhao Zixin. Four supervisory committee members were elected: Hua Shaochun, Ge Zicai, Chen Pinsan, and Cai Yourong. Before the voting, the county party headquarters stated that according to Article 19 of the Chamber of Commerce Law, the term of office for both executive and supervisory committee members is four years. If the term of the current chamber of commerce executive and supervisory committee members has not yet expired and an executive committee member is elected as a supervisory committee member, or a supervisory committee member is elected as an executive committee member during the re-election, would that election be valid? They telegraphed the provincial party headquarters for instructions and clarification. A reply telegram was received stating that if the above situation occurs, it would conflict with the Chamber of Commerce Law and should be declared invalid. The Chamber of Commerce was immediately instructed to act accordingly. However, the Chamber of Commerce believed that the matter concerned the interpretation of laws and regulations and that, according to legislative practice, it should be handled by the central government, not by the provincial or county authorities. They immediately telegraphed the central party headquarters, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry for instructions and clarification. As a result of this ballot count, the newly elected executive committee members included three current supervisory committee members: Qian Sunqing, Cheng Jingdong, and Chen Zhanru. If the provincial telegram is followed, then Wu Bangzhou, Xue Huidong, and Shen Xijun, who were the top three alternates, should fill the vacancies. The current Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to hold a joint meeting of the old and new executive and supervisory committees today (the 18th) to discuss everything. After the ballot results were announced, Qian Sunqing, one of the newly elected executive committee members and a former supervisory committee member, sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce stating that he wished to remain on the supervisory committee and did not wish to be elected as an executive committee member.

Zhenjiang

Winter Relief Begins Distribution

The Zhenjiang Winter Relief Committee has been organized and established for some time. The committee originally planned to begin distribution on the 15th of this month, but due to rain and mud, it was postponed to yesterday. To ensure thoroughness, the city and suburbs were divided into six groups, each led by a group leader and five or six staff members. After gathering at the Chamber of Commerce building at 8:00 AM, they went to their designated locations to distribute aid according to the addresses. Because the area is vast, it was not completed by evening. It is reported that the amount of aid distributed is based on the degree of poverty, divided into four grades: "Heaven," "Earth," "Harmony," and "Peace." The exact amounts for each grade will be determined after the number of households receiving each grade has been tallied.

Dispute Between Two Bookstores Unresolved

Ye Jungu, the manager of the Baicheng Bookstore on Zhongshan Road, previously accused Zhou Renxi and Chen Xianting, the managers of the neighboring Zhonghe Bookstore, of arson with the intention of claiming insurance, harming neighboring stores and causing an innocent loss of over four thousand dollars. Unwilling to accept this, he filed a criminal complaint with the Prosecutor's Office. After the investigation was completed, no prosecution was initiated. Ye refused to accept the judgment and petitioned the High Court for reconsideration, but it was again rejected. Ye, believing that the evidence of the defendant's arson was conclusive, submitted the evidence and exhibits and continued to request reconsideration. Huang Yongzhong, the chief prosecutor of the court, rejected Ye's request, stating that it was not in accordance with the law. It is reported that Ye has now appealed according to law.

Water Patrol Captures Five Bandits

Liu Liancheng, the patrol chief of the Shuigou Town water patrol team stationed in the Third District, received a tip from an informant that bandits were hiding in the town. He immediately led his team to make arrests, capturing bandits Zhu San and Pan Dalang. After interrogation, they confessed to robbing Zhang Zheng Biao, the head of Quanye Village in the district, and the Xu family in Chenjia Xia, as well as implicating five accomplices: Lu Liancai, Peng Fuyang, and Xie Baikui.
