(Shenbao Fourth Sheet)

Educational News

Outlying Areas

Inspector Zhong Daozan of the Ministry of Education Discusses

Inspecting Education in Nanjing

Inspector and Section Chief Zhong Daozan of the Ministry of Education is currently compiling his report on his recent inspection of education in Nanjing. I had the opportunity to speak with him, and he shared his impressions, which are recorded below.

▲ Elementary Education: There are a total of 39 municipal elementary schools in Nanjing, with 15,926 students and a budget of 445,512 yuan. There are a total of 30 municipal compulsory elementary schools, with 5,442 students and a budget of 75,084 yuan. There are a total of 30 registered private elementary schools, with 4,365 students and a budget of 98,400 yuan. There are 16 unregistered private elementary schools, with 1,958 students and a budget of 33,768 yuan. There are 6 public elementary schools run by various institutions, with more than 1,600 students. There are 16 municipal kindergartens, with 888 students, and 5 private kindergartens, with 240 students. In addition, there are 50 to 60 private elementary schools of a church nature whose names are unknown, and the number of students and expenses are unknown. There are also a total of 574 private schools, with 14,995 students. The total expenses of municipal elementary schools, compulsory schools, and private schools amount to 700,000 yuan. Including public elementary schools and private schools of a church nature, the total is nearly 800,000 yuan. Adding the income of private schools, averaging 300 yuan per school, there should be a total of 170,000 yuan. Therefore, the total amount of elementary education expenses in Nanjing exceeds 1 million yuan. Observing this, I feel that the amount of education in Nanjing has increased by 10% compared to before 1932. At the same time, the population has also increased by 10% (Nanjing currently has a population of 730,000). If we calculate based on the general standard that there should be one school-age child for every ten people, then there should be 73,000 students among the 730,000 people. However, this standard is not applicable to Nanjing, because Nanjing is a place where people from all over gather, and many civil servants, military police, and others do not have families and school-age children. Actually, there should be less than 65,000 students. There are currently 48,000 students in school. Although there are still 17,000 out-of-school children, elementary education is more popular than in other prosperous cities.

▲ Secondary Education: There is one municipal secondary school, with 465 students and a budget of 59,892 yuan. There are three public secondary schools (provincial Nanjing Middle School, Nanjing Women's Middle School, and National Central University Experimental School), with 1,560 students and a budget of over 200,000 yuan. There are 14 registered private secondary schools, with 5,846 students and a budget of 549,900 yuan. There are 8 unregistered secondary schools (and several schools for orphans and the ambitious that have not been thoroughly investigated), with 954 students and a budget of 94,752 yuan. The total expenses of public and private schools are approximately 1 million yuan. Most of the secondary schools in the city are ordinary, and the schools run by the government are more numerous than private schools, and the expenses they occupy are more generous than private schools.

▲ Social Education: There are 28 public schools for citizens in Nanjing, with 1,971 students and a budget of 1,705 yuan. There are 14 social education organizations, 24 supplementary schools (including 4 vocational schools), and 48 cultural organizations.

▲ Education Expenses: In 1933, the city's education expenses totaled 683,582 yuan. The allocation for elementary education accounted for slightly less than 77%, for secondary education, slightly less than 11% (vocational education accounted for 24% of secondary education expenses, and middle schools accounted for 76%), and for social education, 76%. The planned budget for the next year (i.e., the 23rd year after the summer) is set at 948,494 yuan. It is planned to allocate slightly more than 74% for elementary education, 13% for secondary education, and 10.13% for social education. Vocational education accounts for 51.5% of secondary education expenses (planning to establish one senior industrial school and two vocational supplementary schools, and one junior vocational school), and middle schools account for 48.5% of secondary education expenses, including three classes for normal schools. This is the result of the consultation between the ministry inspector and the city officials. The city officials plan to proceed according to the budget plan. Whether it can be fully achieved after the summer depends on future facts. Regarding the independence of the city's education expenses, the city government recently designated the Ministry of Finance to provide funds and a portion of the house tax as special funds for education (if there is a shortage, temporary special funds will be designated to supplement). They are deposited into the municipal bank every month and are not used for other purposes. At the same time, a committee for the safekeeping of education funds is jointly organized by the Secretary-General of the City Government, the directors of the Social and Financial Bureaus, and two representatives of middle and elementary school teachers to perform their duties and seek to guarantee the funds.

▲ Education Administration: The authorities of various schools in Nanjing mostly fail to implement the regulations for middle and elementary schools and normal vocational schools promulgated by the Ministry of Education. In particular, regarding the number of students per class, the collection of fees, the number of teaching hours for teachers, the integration of teaching and training, youth guidance, manual labor education, coeducation, administrative organization, and other issues, there are many places that cannot be consistent with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education. Although it is said that there are occasional special difficulties that cannot be fully complied with, it is also an unavoidable fact that they are governed by past habits and do not reform. It is hoped that this can be improved.

▲ Teaching Equipment: A few schools, such as Zhongying, Anhui, and the National Central University Experimental School (the two provincial middle schools were inspected by Councilor Chen, and Zhong did not mention them), all have considerable equipment for science, while the equipment for manual labor education is simple and inadequate, except for the Municipal No. 1 Middle School and the National Central University Experimental School. A few schools even have this subject but no equipment, which is far from the central government's hope for the goal of manual labor education.

▲ Teaching Methods: Teaching methods for various subjects, such as Chinese, English, social studies, and science, mostly adopt lecture and injection methods, failing to use materials and opportunities to allow students to study and work on their own.

▲ Training and Guidance: In terms of training and student guidance, many private secondary schools are affected by financial difficulties and often recruit more students, with 70 or 80 students in each class. By the time they graduate in the third year, the school teachers and staff can hardly do more than recognize the students' names and faces, let alone understand each student's personality, and there are even fewer facilities for academic and career guidance. At the same time, the education administration authorities have failed to actively proceed in accordance with the methods promulgated by the Ministry of Education for academic and career guidance for middle and elementary school students.

▲ Compulsory Education: Municipal compulsory elementary schools are to help out-of-school children and to do a lot with a small amount of money. Generally speaking, the academic performance of students is still passable. However, there are some points that need to be paid attention to: (1) The school buildings and equipment are too simple and crude. (2) The selection of teachers and teaching are not as good as those of ordinary elementary schools. (3) The curriculum focuses on language and mathematics, and the third and fourth grades still adopt a full-day system, which is the same as ordinary elementary schools. Therefore, students have no special difficulties in entering ordinary senior elementary schools. However, they lack a lot in terms of the entire educational life. Most of the senior elementary schools they can enter are not excellent schools above the horizontal line. Therefore, it cannot be considered as evidence of considerable achievement simply because their level can occasionally connect with that of ordinary elementary schools. Therefore, in order to make the academic performance of the compulsory elementary schools excellent, it is necessary to utilize excellent equipment to achieve considerable results. It is definitely not possible for schools with simple and inadequate facilities to express the entire spirit of elementary education. Therefore, the compulsory elementary schools in Nanjing should pay special attention to equipment and teaching in the future.

▲ Corporal Punishment Phenomenon: Many elementary schools practice corporal punishment. Corporal punishment is a kind of educational method in the past that is unnatural and full of inertia, and it is strictly prohibited by law. It must not be allowed to exist. It is hoped that the local education authorities will investigate and prohibit it to avoid the spread of bad habits and affect the development of elementary education.

Chairman He Jian of Hunan

Severe Punishment for a Student Movement

Trial of Military Training for Normal School Students

Order for the Expulsion of the Entire Class

(Changsha Correspondence) Hunan has established a National Military Training Committee, with He Jian serving as its chairman, overseeing military training in provincial secondary and higher-level schools. Students who fail military training will not be allowed to graduate, aiming to rigorously implement military-national education to cope with foreign aggression and seek self-strengthening, with the best of intentions. Each school has appointed a military training director and military training instructors. Over the past year, while considerable achievements have been made, disputes have also arisen repeatedly. For example, students from Hunan University and the Qunzhi Law School mostly refuse to accept military training, claiming that they do not want to be warlords and therefore do not need military training. The biggest reason is that those serving as military training directors and instructors, apart from military matters, lack sufficient knowledge to inspire the students' faith and are often despised by the students, so they are unwilling to be trained by them. Students from the Provincial First Middle School also disapprove of military training for the same reasons. Recently, the National Military Training Committee, because the military training of the ninth class of normal school students was about to conclude, specially sent Committee Member Kuang Shushu to the school to conduct the military training graduation examination. Student number twenty was caught cheating, and when Kuang stopped him, he refused to comply. The whole class suddenly erupted in an uproar, tearing up their papers and refusing to take the exam, shouting and yelling loudly. Kuang fled in a panic and reported to the National Military Training Committee, which convened a temporary emergency meeting to decide on a solution: (1) Expel all students of the ninth class of the school; (2) For the ringleaders, expel them, and for the rest of the class, record demerits and allow them to remain in school under observation for a year; (3) Record demerits for the entire class and allow them to remain in school under observation. After the above resolutions were made, they were reported to He Jian for approval. He Jian, in order to rigorously implement military training and rectify academic standards, adopted the first option, ordering the expulsion of the entire class to serve as a warning. At the same time, Wu Huihua, the principal of the First Middle School, immediately convened a meeting to give a lecture after the students boycotted the examination, explaining the greater significance. The students were all able to repent and, with all students signing and stamping, submitted a letter of repentance, requesting leniency and promising to absolutely accept military training examinations in the future. Zhu Jingnong, the Director of the Education Department, then took the students' letter of repentance to meet with He Jian, explaining the students' subsequent repentance and requesting that the second and third options proposed by the National Military Training Committee be adopted to show compassion. This was because the students in the class had been studying at the school for five years since starting junior high school, and they would be graduating in June of this year. Expelling the entire class would be a regrettable outcome. Unfortunately, He Jian's mind was already made up, and there was no way to reverse the decision. Director Zhu had no choice but to implement the plan, ordering on the 13th that all forty-odd young people in the class be expelled. (January 13th)

Henan Province Middle School Entrance Exam Begins

Jinan Correspondence: The third annual graduation examination for middle school students in the province, divided into thirteen districts across the province, began on the 16th. The Jinan district examination venue is located at the Provincial First Normal School. There are 294 examinees, and He Siyuan, Director of the Education Department, is serving concurrently as the chief examiner. The supervising committee members are Lee Chin-ho, a prosecutor representing the High Court, and Yang Wen-fu, a section chief representing the Municipal Government. There are eleven examination rooms in the venue, with the seating arrangements already determined and properly arranged. Starting at 7:30 AM, thirteen of the examinees did not arrive, with 281 students present (including 14 girls from middle school). Their names were called, and they were given exam papers and entered the venue in order. In the Jinan district, only mathematics is being re-examined for senior high school students, and there is no re-examination for junior high school students. The graduation examination is entirely for junior high school students. Although nearly 300 people took the exam today, the order was well maintained. All staff members wore red ribbons and were under strict surveillance. From 8:00 AM to 12:15 PM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, the exam was completed. It will continue on the following day.

Local News

Hainan Biological Collection Group

Yesterday, in Two Batches, Passed Through Shanghai to the South

▲ Organized by Seven Groups, with a Total of Twelve Members

▲ The Land and Sea Teams Plan to Collect for One Year

The Hainan Biological Collection Group, jointly organized by seven groups including the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China, departed from Shanghai to the south in two batches the day before yesterday. The details are as follows:

Founding Organizations: The Hainan Biological Collection Group was originally initiated and organized by six groups, including the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China, the Natural History Museum of the Academia Sinica, the Jing Sheng Biological Survey Institute of Beiping, Peking University, Tsinghua University, and Shandong University. Later, the Guangzhou Geological Survey Institute was introduced by the Beiping Geological Survey Institute to participate, so the group is jointly organized by seven groups.

List of Members: The group has twelve members, and the list is as follows: (1) He Qi from the Jing Sheng Biological Survey Institute (Entomology), Tang Shankang (Taxidermist), Xing Huayan and Feng Lian'ge (Technicians); (2) Liu Cheng from Shandong University (Anthropology), Zuo Jinglie (Botany), and Li Yugui (School Worker); (3) Wang Yikang from the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China (Ichthyology), Liu Zhibie and Zhang Zongjun (Technicians); (4) Tang Jufeng from the Natural History Museum of the Academia Sinica (Marine Animals) and Deng Xiangkun (Lower Plants). Zuo Jinglie is the team leader, and Wang Yikang is the deputy team leader.

Departure in Two Batches: The group of twelve members came to Shanghai from Beijing the day before yesterday and stayed at the Huizhong Hotel. The first batch, including Tang Shankang, Xing Huayan, Feng Lian'ge, Li Yugui, Liu Zhibie, Zhang Zongjun, and Deng Xiangkun, took a steamer south the night before yesterday. Zuo Jinglie, He Qi, Liu Xian, Wang Yikang, and Tang Shifeng departed on the Japanese Empress of the Changxing Company to Hong Kong last night.

Collection Plan: According to team leader Zuo Jinglie's interview with reporters yesterday, there have been several organizations of Chinese biological collection groups, but they have all departed to collect in Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guangxi. The only one collecting in Hainan is Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou, but they are limited to higher plants, and this group is the first to consider all parts. In addition to investigating higher plants, lower plants, and animals, this departure will also focus on anthropology. There are many Miao and Li people in Hainan, which is very important for human relations. The collection will be divided into land and sea teams. The sea team will specialize in collecting marine organisms, and the land team will be divided into mountain and land groups to specialize in collecting animals, plants, and anthropology.

One-Year Deadline: Zuo also said that the planned deadline for this departure is one year. They are carrying more than 30 pieces of equipment, medicines, and camping gear, and will go to Guangzhou to wait for a boat to Hainan. The cost is 8,000 yuan, which is shared by the four groups. The first step after returning with the collected materials is to distribute the collected materials to various institutions for research, and the second step is to combine the research results and then distribute them to various institutions for teaching materials and other references.

City Education Bureau

Continuing Wireless Radio Broadcasting Education

▲ From the 16th of this Month, 8:00 AM to 9:00 AM

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued a notice to continue wireless radio broadcasting education, stating that to facilitate the acquisition of knowledge and skills for long-term dropouts, the Bureau has now agreed with the Fuxing Radio Station to continue broadcasting educational programs such as [English] and [Chinese] from 8:00 AM to 9:00 AM daily (except Sundays), starting on January 16th. Xie Fusheng will be hired to broadcast English on Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays, and lectures will be compiled with textbooks, which will be distributed by the Shanghai Morning Post on a regular basis in two publications called [English Broadcasting Weekly] [each issue retails for five cents, and a full year of 50 issues costs two yuan]. On Tuesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays, Bao Renjie will broadcast Chinese, using the second volume of the Contemporary Chinese Language textbook for junior high school students published by the Shanghai Middle School Student Bookstore. Students attending lectures should prepare their own textbooks. Those who wish to study English and Chinese can listen to the lectures on the radio at the scheduled times. The radio station's wavelength is 920 kilocycles. This notice is hereby issued for general information.

To Safeguard Important Jinan University Documents

(Shanghai News) The turmoil at National Jinan University surrounding the expulsion of Zheng has not yet been resolved. The City Education Bureau yesterday sent personnel to the school to work with the Expel Zheng Association to safeguard important documents. The Shanghai Alumni Association also sent representatives to petition Mayor Wu and Director Pan. The details are as follows:

Xiong Pengnan, a representative of the association, received him. As a result of the consultations, the important documents of the Registrar's Office were sealed.

▲ Representatives Petitioning in Beijing Telegraph Success: The Expel Zheng Association received a telegram from the representatives of the school petitioning in Beijing, stating that the process in Beijing is going smoothly and that all parties are expressing great sympathy. The issue of removing Zheng will be resolved at the Fourth Plenary Session.

▲ Shanghai Alumni Association Calls on Mayor Wu: The Shanghai Alumni Association sent representatives Qiu Hanping, Qiu Zhizhong, Xie Huaiqing, Lan Wenhai, and Li Jialin to call on Mayor Wu yesterday morning to report on the establishment of the association and the truth of the turmoil, and to request that he forward a letter to the Municipal Party Headquarters to prevent the activities of the previously dismissed committee members. The mayor personally received them and promised to go to Beijing within a few days to discuss the issue of the principal with the school board members. The representatives then went to the City Education Bureau to call on Director Pan, requesting that the details of the expulsion of Zheng at Jinan University be forwarded to the Ministry of Education. Director Pan agreed to handle the matter. The representatives then returned to the association.

New Look for the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School

The Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School in this city has been established for thirteen years. Hundreds of students have graduated and are serving the cause of women's physical education in various provinces of China and the Nanyang Islands. In recent years, the school has been striving to advance its operations and improve the campus environment. In the winter of the 20th year of the Republic, it rented its newly built buildings on Daji Road to the Aiqun Girls' Middle School and opened a new campus base of dozens of acres in Jiangwan. Unexpectedly, after just moving in, it was hit by the January 28th Incident, and all facilities were destroyed, with losses amounting to tens of thousands. However, the school's principal, Ms. Lu Lihua, did not let this dampen her spirits. With the spirit of accepting adversity, she struggled independently, 13 years as one day. Last autumn, the Jiangwan site was rebuilt for the second time, investing heavily in various sports fields, gyms, and all facilities to make them perfect. It is said that a large track and field and a dormitory that can accommodate more than 200 students will be built during this winter vacation. It is expected to be completed by the start of the school year. It is also planned to start building a gymnasium and swimming pool in the spring of this year, which is expected to be completed within two years to create a large-scale women's physical education school.

Fuller School for the Deaf Adds School Buildings

The Fuller School for the Deaf on Jessfield Road, Kangding Bridge in this city, was founded by Dr. Brown, an American missionary, and has achieved outstanding results. Most of the teachers it hires are experts from Yantai who have studied for many years and have broad and rich academic knowledge and experience. In particular, it uses phonetic symbols, Roman letters, and Bailey letters as pronunciation symbols to teach deaf students, which is its only characteristic. Because the number of applicants has been increasing, the original school buildings, classrooms, and dormitories are not enough. Two new buildings have been added in a lane a few steps away. The old and new buildings together are large enough to accommodate more than 100 people, and many new teachers have been hired.

Two Rivers Overcomes the Red Team

As the game between the Two Rivers and Red teams began, the atmosphere instantly became tense. Ministry of Education's Physical Education Curriculum Outline

Detailed Record of the Drafting Committee Meeting

The Drafting Committee for the Ministry of Education's Physical Education Curriculum Outline for Primary and Secondary Schools continued its meeting on the 16th from 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM. Attending were Wu Yunrui, Song Junfu, Cheng Dengke, Chen Kuisheng, Hao Gengsheng, Wu Ji, Ling Chen Yingmei, Guo Lianfeng, and others, chaired by Hao Gengsheng. The following resolutions were made:

Division of Labor

(1) The Physical Education Goals proposal was passed with revisions. (2) The types of teaching materials for each grade and their allocation methods were passed with revisions. (3) The document format proposal was resolved to use blank spaces and new punctuation marks, printed vertically, with the sections used arranged as [Chapter] [Section] [　] [一] [(一)] [(丨)]. (4) The proposal to change the Physical Education Curriculum Outline to a Physical Education Detailed Outline was passed. (5) The work allocation proposal was resolved with Chen Yingmei and Chen Kuisheng responsible for editing the primary school section, Wu Yunrui and Song Junfu responsible for editing the junior high school section, and Cheng Dengke and Wu (blank space) responsible for editing the senior high school section. (6) The deadline for submission proposal was resolved with the deadline for the primary school section at the end of May, the junior high school section at the end of March, and the senior high school section at the end of June. All manuscripts should be submitted to the chief editor Wu Yunrui for review. (7) The issue of physical education equipment was resolved that schools with sufficient resources should strictly follow the requirements of the National Physical Education Implementation Plan for equipment. Those unable to do so should, at a minimum, equip themselves according to the detailed items compiled by the committee. It was also heard that the detailed items would be printed in three large volumes for primary, junior, and senior high schools, each estimated to be over 120,000 words. The passed physical education goals are recorded below:

Physical Education Goals

(A) Primary School: (1) Develop the functions of the internal and external organs of children's bodies to promote appropriate overall development. (2) Adapt to children's inherent love of activity and develop their athletic abilities to cultivate the athletic skills needed for daily life and national defense. (3) Cultivate children's courage, agility, endurance, honesty, fairness, cheerfulness, sacrifice, service, law-abidingness, cooperation, mutual assistance, and patriotism to prepare them for restoring the nation, resisting insults, and defending against enemies. (4) Develop a habit of enjoying sports to create a foundation for proper entertainment. (B) Junior High School: (1) Strengthen the physique and ensure healthy physical and mental development to prepare for revitalizing the nation, resisting enemies, and defending against aggression. (2) Cultivate obedience, endurance, self-governance, loyalty, courage, cooperation, law-abidingness, mutual assistance, patriotism, and other civic virtues through team sports. (3) Cultivate the athletic skills needed for daily life and national defense. (4) Develop a habit of using sports as proper entertainment. (C) Senior High School: (1) Continue to strengthen the physique and ensure healthy physical and mental development to implement the revitalization of the nation, resist insults, and defend against enemies to seek national survival. (2) Continue to cultivate patriotism and train civic virtues through team sports. (3) Cultivate the athletic skills needed for life and military affairs. (4) Develop a habit of using sports as proper entertainment.

Spring and Autumn

Wishing for a Sign of a Lean Year

— Yan Qiao

Snow is a sign of a bountiful year, so every year there is snow, and every year the autumn harvest is abundant. Who knew that despite the annual bumper harvests, farmers still clamor about being poor every year? What is the reason for this? We only hear farmers talking about "ripe wasteland." Ripe and wasteland are relative terms; how can they be linked together to form a noun? We don't understand economics; there are those who do who can expound grand theories. I wonder when their grand theories will have an impact on farmers? When will farmers' actual lives be able to improve a bit?

A few days ago, this damn snow came down again, blanketing the sky. Naturally, from a scientific standpoint, it's also a harbinger of good fortune, freezing all the pests to death, guaranteeing another year of good harvest. I'm afraid next year will still have the word "wasteland" attached to "ripe," spat out from the frustrated tone of the haggard farmers.

Yuan Sheng, in his "Old Study Cong Tan" of the Zizhai Studio, said that Jia Sidao, because there was no snow in the twelfth month, and the wheat couldn't grow, lit candles and burned incense at the fifth watch, silently praying to the heavens. That day, before noon, clouds rose and there was light rain, and at dusk it snowed, and it fell heavily at night, accumulating several inches at the second watch. At the third watch, an imperial plaque was issued, praising the timely snow and the answered prayers. That semi-retired prime minister was so patriotic and loved the people, and the heavens actually responded. Mr. Sheng's words are a bit too saccharine; he doesn't know that even if the auspicious snow came in time, the Yuan soldiers still penetrated deep into the country.

In this era of revolution and science, naturally no one is willing to talk about auspicious omens anymore. Who knew that those local newspapers in the inland areas, which bear the responsibility of guiding public opinion, would actually write about "auspicious snow"? We not only felt nauseous, but also a bit heartbroken. If the Japanese saw heavy snow in the three northeastern provinces, it would be fitting for them to call it auspicious snow. As for foreshadowing a bountiful year, I'm afraid it's not what 70% of Chinese farmers hope for. Because they would rather have a bad harvest and higher rice prices, which would be more beneficial to them. I heard a farmer say this myself. What kind of psychology is this?

This year's snow fell quickly, accumulated quickly, and melted quickly. From beginning to end, it lasted less than twelve hours. One moment, it seemed like jade buildings and silver palaces, and the next, it was back to the same old shack and leaky roof. This can be taken as a symbol of the Fujian Incident.

Year-End Sorrow

— Du Yun

A certain day's business in a large bookstore on the Fourth Road amounted to only one dollar and two cents.

Waking up early in the morning, I heard that someone had hanged himself under a small tree at the corner of Baochang Road. Driven by curiosity, I went to watch. The body was still hanging from the tree, looking like a small businessman in his forties, wearing a used overcoat bought on the stone road, his hat fallen on the ground, his face pale, his mouth and eyes half-open. A large crowd gathered to watch, irresponsibly speculating, "He must have committed suicide because he couldn't bear the cold weather, the approaching end of the year, the suffering from hunger and cold, and the creditors' demands. Alas! What a pity!"

When you walk past the area near North Sichuan Road and Laobazi Road at around 9 PM, someone will forcibly pull you in to taste Western-style meat; you will also faintly hear shouts of "Three Dollars Only! Only three dollars is enough!"

In a shoe store on North Henan Road that is preparing to close, two comedic partners are standing at the entrance. Although they are slapping shoe soles in their hands and shouting about big discounts, very few people enter to buy cheap goods!

A seller of glutinous rice rolls told me that in previous years he could sell twenty or thirty thousand cash every morning, but now only three or four thousand, with a profit of two cents, not even enough for a day's expenses.

A certain cinema only had three viewers for one night show.

A barber is also sighing, "Maybe this year is colder than in previous years! Why are people afraid to come for a haircut?"

Even famous paintings and calligraphy are no longer valuable in this situation. There are fewer people appreciating them than in previous years, and collectors are as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns!

Big discounts, winter discounts, genuine, extraordinary, special, honest, sacrifices, painful sales, clearance sales, shop closures, all kinds of big discounts, bright flags waving, ear-splitting military music playing, all of this, all of it, expresses nothing but the sorrow of the year's end.

Talking About Heavenly Bamboo

— Yi Mei

Heavenly bamboo sprigs inserted in vases are, along with wintersweet and daffodils, exquisite products of the cold season. Also known as Southern Heavenly Candle, or abbreviated as Heavenly Bamboo, it is an evergreen shrub commonly found in the Wu and Chu regions. The tree grows three to five feet tall, occasionally reaching ten feet, but it is not easy to see. Furthermore, the taller ones do not bear fruit. The leaves resemble those of the chinaberry but are smaller, and they do not wither in winter. Small white flowers with five petals bloom in March and April, and the berries grow in clusters, gradually turning red like cinnabar in winter, which is very lovely when set against the snow. There are many variations, with flowers that are crimson in color and berries that are either yellow or white. It prefers shade and dislikes dampness, making it ideal for planting in courtyards or against walls. Mound it with yellow mud, and it will naturally thrive. Do not water it with manure; if you must water it, use cold tea or water infused with pheasant or magpie feathers. Respectfully prune its trunk in autumn, leaving only the solitary root, and side branches will grow, making it short and suitable for bonsai, a refined offering for a scholar's studio. Heavenly bamboo is like a beautiful woman of old, charming and lovely, and also like a refined scholar, elegant and free from vulgarity. Unfortunately, I live in cramped quarters with no space to plant it, and I am constantly moving. Otherwise, I would plant lush branches and leaves, with one or two jagged rocks nearby. Looking at them would make me forget the world and dispel worries. There would be no need to retire from the world, and I would naturally find the pleasure of seclusion in the mountains and forests. At the end of the year and the beginning of the new year, around Huajinli and Ermalu in Shanghai, sellers of daffodils, wintersweet, and heavenly bamboo gather to form a market. However, many people are deceitful, inserting already fallen berries into the branches. They may seem pleasingly red, but when purchased and brought home, the berries soon wither and turn black. Careful examination is essential to avoid being fooled.

Although Zhang Zixiang is famous for painting peonies, his other bamboo, rocks, orchids, and chrysanthemums are also exceptional and refined, highly regarded by people. One day, he was making a screen, depicting the four seasons, spring, summer, autumn, and winter. When he reached the last panel, he suddenly had a dispute with his wife over a trivial matter. His wife, in anger, threw his painting tools on the ground to vent her anger. The fat from the lamp splashed and spilled onto the painting, with countless dots. Zixiang quickly took up his brush and turned it into a cluster of heavenly bamboo, with a special artistic touch, far superior to his usual work. From then on, there was a steady stream of requests for him to paint heavenly bamboo as a background element, greatly improving his livelihood.

A Certain Blind Man (Part 2)

— Hui Jian

The blind man's forehead was filled with bulging blue veins from anger. He walked up to Mr. Liu Si in fury and said in a cold voice, "Everyone is like this; everyone loves to inquire, and yet no one is willing to believe. Why would Xu Lao Jiu deceive me? He is my best friend. He has been hoping for someone to cure my blindness for over a decade. Five years ago, he told me the name of Ma Keli Sha. He spoke with such sincerity! Pour some yellow liquid from a silver medicine bottle and dab it on my eyelids, that's all, he said. I won't forget a single word he said. Why would he deceive me? Let me tell you, Ma Keli Sha really exists..."

Mr. Liu Si originally wanted to say, "Because Xu Lao Jiu is your good friend, that's why he deceived you," but he clearly knew that saying those words would shatter the blind man's heart. He immediately said with a gentle laugh, "You are truly brave, but I think Ma Keli Sha may already be very old now."

The blind man said calmly, "Yes, if he is alive, he would be seventy-two years old this year, but I still want to find him. I have been looking for him for five years."

He accompanied the blind man across a river that was the furthest from his village. Across the river was the territory of another village. He watched as the blind man's faltering figure gradually faded and disappeared into that distant, unreachable horizon, and he imagined him stopping every passerby, asking in his strange, gloomy voice that would annoy anyone who heard it, "Please tell me, is Mr. Ma Keli Sha still alive?"

Mr. Liu Si would never forgive Xu Lao Jiu for this extraordinary sin.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23

Unbearable Pain Heedfully Listens to Music Joyful Sentiment Not Yet Sated Prompt Separation with Urgent Message

As Ji Zhi saw him, he also had a bit of humility, so he poured a cup of tea, lowered his head, and slowly sipped it. While he was sipping the tea, Zhao Weng said a few words intentionally or unintentionally, but Ji Zhi didn't hear them, only lowering his head to drink the tea. Zhao Weng watched him with cold eyes and said nothing, putting his hands behind his back, walking back and forth in the open space, looking up slightly, only watching the red leaves on the mountain. They remained like this for about half an hour, neither of them speaking. Zhao Weng walked back to his seat and smiled at Ji Zhi, "Second Master, let's return after enjoying ourselves, we don't need to go up the mountain anymore, we can find two animals and slowly go back." Ji Zhi stood up and smiled, "We have been sitting here for too long, it's probably too late to go up the mountain, it's good to go back together." So he took out money to pay for the tea, and the two walked to the foot of the mountain, hired two donkeys, and walked back along the road. After walking about four or five miles, two or three cars chased them from behind. The ground on this road had been crushed by large carts and was originally a very thick layer of loose soil. Now, as the cars sped past on the loose soil, plumes of dust flew up, obscuring people's eyes and ears. Ji Zhi saw that there was an officer in the car, with two young women on either side of him. He turned his head to one side, coughed for a while, and walked a hundred steps before the flying dust settled. He laughed on the donkey's back, "Old Master, did you see that? The people in the car are the same ones who were hugging women and having fun in the Xishan Inn upstairs just now. Do you believe that these people can save the country and the people?" Zhao Weng sighed, "Alas! There's no way to deal with this." Ji Zhi smiled, "Let me tell a joke, please don't be angry. When Zhao Company Commander becomes a division commander or army commander in the future, you must tell him not to learn from these officers." Zhao Weng said, "You're right. When people have no money or power, you can't see any bad qualities, but once they have money and power, all kinds of bad habits come out. But my boy, as far as I know, is still honest, but I can't say for sure in the future. But even if there are army commanders and division commanders, it won't be his turn." (294)

Miscellaneous Talk

Talking About Snow

— Zhu Ji

After a few warm days and one night of north wind, snow, like flying catkins and spreading cotton, flew all over the sky. A silver light covered all the heights and roughness of the world; the houses were adorned with jade and wrapped in silver, the mountains and forests were piled with jade powder, everything in the human world became bright and pure. Standing on a high building and looking out, it was truly jade palaces and silver towers, a single color for ten thousand miles! The superficial embellishment of the world is called "whitewashing peace," but human power is ultimately not as great as nature! Only snow can whitewash everything, can create a flat scene between heaven and earth!

Stories about snow, like Sun Kang reading by the light of snow, Wang Ziyou visiting Dai An in the snowy night, and Meng Haoran looking for plum blossoms in the snow, are all famous and recorded in history. Sun Kang, this kind of bookworm, is said to be a headache for school authorities nowadays. Wang Ziyou's unique temperament is also impractical now. Only the elegant and profound taste of the old master Meng is the most popular, and it is enough to be modern. Please see that in the near future, in front of the tomb of the recluse Lin Bu, in the Dengwei Fragrant Snow Sea, a continuous stream of important people and celebrities, Fujian talents and men of letters will come to look for plum blossoms and walk in the snow, to adorn this beautiful country.

Due to the eastward flow of European winds, as Christmas approaches, ordinary new-style stores also decorate a seasonal snow scene in the glass windows, to show their understanding of the times. A group of modern girls, to show their Westernization, will also enthusiastically express themselves in the park's north wind by building snowmen and chasing snowballs, things that they wouldn't have glanced at before. Unfortunately, this grand event has not yet spread to the inland areas. The snowmen piled up in the streets and alleys of Suzhou are still the original art of the children, and they are not very ingenious. However, the snow lion in front of a certain Buddhist store last year was majestic and imposing; unfortunately, this kind of artwork was only appreciated by a few children, and as soon as the sun came out, it quickly melted away with the flowing water, leaving no trace.

Santa Claus is a kind, red-robed, white-bearded old man. He often secretly gives people the things they need in the snow, especially children, who are the only recipients of his gifts. On Christmas morning, when children wake up from their sweet dreams, the things they have been waiting for all year are already hanging high in their socks. Therefore, European and American children regard Santa Claus as their only beloved benefactor. Although this is a myth used by Europeans and Americans to coax children, Christmas is always a happy day for foreigners, just like the lunar New Year in our country. But now that our country's society and economy are gradually collapsing, people's attitude towards the New Year is like Wang Xiaoer's New Year, very difficult. If there really is a Santa Claus in the world, I really wish he would visit China once, like Bernard Shaw, and send some gifts to the people. Unfortunately, the economies of Europe and America are mostly preoccupied with their own affairs. My ideal is only like looking at this powder-like white snow, unable to really turn into powder to relieve human hunger.

Snow is a hexagonal crystal, so Chinese people call snow "Teng Liugong." The Elementary Learning says that snow flies in six petals, a harbinger of a bountiful year. According to ancient tradition, winter snow can kill common pests that harm plants. It is said that the more snow falls, the more those hibernating pests cannot resist the cold and are completely frozen to death. When plants sprout in the coming spring, the pests are already dead, and the plants thrive and grow without any insects eating them. Naturally, the five grains will be abundant, and the year will be very prosperous. Therefore, snow can predict the abundance or leanness of the coming year, but the effect of spring snow is the opposite of that of winter snow, so although they are both white snow, their effects are completely different.

When I was young, I saw a story about snow that was profound in meaning and gave the wealthy people who did not know poverty a deep cut. The story said that in a certain year in the state of Qi, there was heavy snow, and Duke Huan of Qi was living in the deep palace with a blazing fire, not feeling the cold at all. He was surprised and asked Yan Pingzhong, "This is really strange, it has been snowing for three days in a row, but I don't feel cold at all, what is the reason for this?" Yan Pingzhong replied well, "Your Majesty lives in the warm palace, drinking lamb wine, naturally you don't feel cold, but how many ordinary people outside have already frozen to death?" People living in waterfront houses, please think about this story when appreciating the snow.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

Japanese Goods in the Women's National Products Year

— Yang Bian

What are the results of the Women's National Products Year? We haven't seen them yet, but the startling newspapers are full of headlines saying, "[Amidst the promotion of national products, the import of inferior goods has greatly increased, reaching over 50,000 tons in just two weeks, with four times more being directly shipped to North China]."

Recently, the Japanese government, seeing the decline of the Chinese anti-Japanese goods movement, has organized a trade control agency for China, with the Japan-China Trade Co., Ltd. as the main body, directly under the guidance of the Director of the Commercial Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and its commercial officials. Its organizational content: (1) Establish a head office in Osaka, Japan. (2) Jointly handle export trade to China by various companies engaged in trade with China and commercial organizations in China. (3) Open branches in Tianjin, Qingdao, Hankou, Fuzhou, Shanghai, and Hong Kong to manage trade within their respective regions. (4) The Director of the Commercial Bureau will appoint a general manager and closely liaise with commercial officials stationed in China to cooperate in controlling the export of goods and developing new markets. (5) Transportation agencies will also be unified and directly managed by the company. (6) Increase the number of commercial officials stationed in inland China to investigate the inland market and find ways to develop it. Such a vicious tactic is attacking us right at the beginning of the Women's National Products Year. How can we resist it with our immature national products industry? We should know that this is not just a matter of life and death for the national products industry; it is a matter of life and death for our entire nation. We have nothing else now but to consistently use national products to save the country and save ourselves. Everyone should recognize that using national products is the starting point of national morality and the foundation of national revival. The women's community has an unshirkable responsibility, and the men are even more obligated. Not only should men and women be united and cooperate fully, but the government and the people must also be sincere and earnest in supporting each other. Tao Jun Leqin once told a reporter, "[To control the economy, one must first start by controlling import and export trade. If import and export trade cannot be controlled, no matter what kind of control you promote, it will be useless]." This statement is very insightful. I believe that the government today, seeing the rapid advance of Japan's control of trade with China, must not engage in empty talk, act hypocritically, or shy away from economic resistance against Japan, thereby leading itself to ruin. Mr. Gu Tinglin said, "[The rise and fall of the world are the responsibility of every man and woman]." Citizens! Citizens! At this critical juncture of life and death, let us no longer stand by, no longer shirk responsibility, no longer be indifferent, and no longer be forgetful. Please see if we can save ourselves this year?

Admit to Half the Blame

— Shen Airong

This year is the [Women's National Products Year]. Gentlemen, take a step back for now and let us women handle it. The play has just begun. Can the leading ladies maintain their consistency and dedication to perform well and achieve a satisfactory result, earning applause from the audience? This, of course, depends on the efforts of the women!

In the past, people ||mostly gentlemen|| always blamed women for not being patriotic and for being happy to promote enemy goods, as if the underdevelopment of Chinese industry was entirely due to women's sabotage. Recently, there was a report of a 900 million yuan trade deficit, with women's goods accounting for the majority, giving the gentlemen a big handle to constantly nag about the women's shortcomings.

I don't deny that women love to be pretty, with rosy faces and colorful clothes, but to insist that women are not patriotic, at least I, as one of the women, am not willing to silently accept this.

Speaking within the small scope of my school, this year the female students' leather coats are all made to order or purchased at the Penglai Market, which shows that the women have some awareness. However, I dare not guarantee whether the wool used to make these coats is domestic.

Rural women who come to Shanghai to buy clothing materials always like to go to Xiaodongmen because it is both cheap and good-looking, but the source of these beautiful and inexpensive fabrics is heartbreaking; most of them are enemy goods. However, the women are not at fault! These fabric stores are all opened by our esteemed compatriots. Some customers, fearing being deceived, ask if the goods are domestic. The answer is not only that they are domestic but also that there is a trademark from a certain factory as evidence, so you can't help but believe it. Women with weak discernment, especially those from the countryside who come to Shanghai, how can they know the secrets within? ||Even the gentlemen probably wouldn't know!||

The gentlemen are the most fond of nitpicking. When they see women dressed attractively, they insist that they are not patriotic. Is wearing a coarse cloth shirt the only way to be called patriotic? Then wearing Lao Jiuhe's domestic silks and satins, wearing leather coats bought at the Penglai Market are all unpatriotic, all regarded as enemy goods? Isn't that a bit too much?

In short, everyone should admit to half the blame. The women must truly live up to the name and not disappoint the [Women's National Products Year]. The gentlemen in the business community should also put their conscience in the right place and not let the sight of silver turn their patriotic red heart black.

Hoping for a Few Women

— Xiao Bai

Along with the opening of the [Women's National Products Year], the tide of [Women Promoting National Products] has spread throughout our society and country. At present, it has become the most important and practical work for our national women's community, like the sun and moon in the sky and rivers on the earth. For the future of revitalizing national products and blocking foreign goods, there will certainly be significant achievements. However, in my humble opinion, there are a few women in our community who, due to special reasons, can guide the public and influence society. Therefore, we must hope that they will be the pioneers, so that the whole country will follow suit, and its effectiveness will naturally be greater. Now, I will list a few that I can think of:

1. Movie stars. Movies have the greatest influence on society, and the actions of movie stars have an even greater impact on the public. Starting this year, if our national movie stars can take the lead in promoting and using national products, and if domestic films can all have performances promoting national products, like the background of [Spring Silkworms] [Perfume Beauty], using the economic invasion of imperialism and women's fondness for foreign goods, which leads to the outflow of money and the decline of domestic products, with the most painful and intense ending, to touch the heartstrings of our national women and promote the determination to love and use national products, the gains will be self-evident.

2. University and middle school students. In recent years, students in universities and middle schools across the country have often liked to wear foreign goods, especially female students, who wear fancy clothes and strange attire. Looking at their clothing, there is no trace of national products. This trend is truly heartbreaking. Starting this year, they must fundamentally awaken and use national products, and teachers must stipulate that all school documents and books, whether uniforms or casual clothes, must use national products; otherwise, once discovered, they will be ordered to drop out of school. Teachers and students should unite and engage in the movement to promote national products.

3. Leaders of women's communities. One call from a leader will be followed by thousands. Whether they are in the political, banking, education, or any other professional field, as well as famous and virtuous women, this year, of course, we must hope that they will take responsibility, use national products, and take the lead in promotion, so that the whole country will follow suit.

The responsibility of promoting national products belongs to everyone. This year is the [Women's National Products Year], and we women must naturally work harder. The people I listed above have a responsibility and cannot shirk it. Of course, they must work hard, be courageous, and strive to move forward on a road full of vitality.

National Products and Modern Women

— Li Qiu

From last year's [National Products Year] to this year's [Women's National Products Year], the cry to promote national products has finally reached the clouds. Although what we see objectively is still a large amount of [trade deficit] and the sluggish production and sales of national products, we cannot deny the great efforts we have made subjectively, which have already established a considerable foundation in the call to promote national products.

This year is the Women's National Products Year. This illustrates that the responsibility of promoting national products is not only borne by men but also must be borne by women as the center of this task. Therefore, every Chinese woman standing on the stage of the Women's National Products Year should make the greatest determination to actually strive to promote national products, so that the meaning of this Women's National Products Year will be richer and more substantial.

Currently, modern women generally wear famous brands from Paris and London, apply foreign cosmetics worth dozens of yuan a box on their faces, and worry that everything they use daily, from shoes and hats to even a small handbag, is not a foreign product, as if it is not modern if it is not a foreign product, and not fashionable if it is not an imported product. The amount of money they spend seems to be irrelevant to them, and they are even more unaware of the loss to national interests!

This year's Women's National Products Year, first of all, we must draw the attention of these modern women. We must make the greatest effort to correct this incorrect trend. We must point out that the modernity and fashion expressed by foreign goods are not true modernity and true fashion. This expression shows one's own ignorance, and in the call to promote national products, it is a shameful behavior!

True modernity and fashion are the love of national products expressed from that pure and high intellect. Although national products are not as good as foreign products in some aspects, if a woman uses national products and wears national products, then the modernity and fashion in her wearing and decoration are enough to show her love for the country and the nation, and to show that she is a modern woman with knowledge and reason. In the call to promote national products, the meaning of modernity should be reinterpreted from the ground up.

No matter if you are wearing the most fashionable clothes of 1934 or using the most expensive popular Parisian cosmetics, because they are not national products, they are not modern!

Only women who use national products are truly modern women!

Mr. Song said to his wife with a smile, "This year is the [Women's National Products Year]. You are wearing all national products, and you can be called a pioneer of modern women."

An Iron Lesson

— Ms. Zhihua

One evening, several guests were sitting in Mr. Li's house, one was Wu Liang, the manager of the Xiezong Department Store, and the other was Wen Lianfu, a university professor.

The conversation began in a very natural way.

"Hey, Brother Wu Liang... I heard that Old Wang's wife is now the chairman of the Women's National Products Movement Committee. Is that true?"

"Of course! But these women are just using this to show off! What can she do?" Wu Liang replied.

"I even saw her giving a speech at the General Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday!"

"Giggle! Giggle!" A burst of laughter ended this short conversation.

×　　×　　×　　×

"The Women's National Products Year has begun, and there is a citywide car parade! The streets and alleys are full of enthusiastic women promoting national products. Mrs. Wang is the general director of the car parade. The wives of Wen Lianfu and Wu Liang are also crowded in the enthusiastic crowd promoting national products.

Passionate speeches. Snowflakes of flyers.

"Resist foreign goods!" "Promote national products!" In the heart of every woman, a passionate national and state view was ignited. The pain of January 28th throbbed in their minds! ×　　×　　×　　×

The next day, the following news was published in the newspaper.

"The Xiezong Department Store in this city has been an agent for the dumping of Japanese goods. It usually buys Japanese goods at low prices and sells them under the trademarks of domestic factories. It was recently discovered by the Seventh Investigation Team of the Women's National Products Movement Committee, which immediately sent personnel to search and found many kinds of original Japanese goods in the warehouse. The committee members, with conclusive evidence, unanimously resolved to confiscate the company in the near future and use it as a national salvation fund, etc."

×　　×　　×　　×

A few days later, there was another announcement in the newspaper...

"Lawyer Shi Mingli, representing Ms. Zhang Yongzhen, issued a statement announcing her divorce from Wu Liang, the manager of Xiezong Company... According to our client, Ms. Zhang Yongzhen, she and Mr. Wu Liang became husband and wife seven years ago through a friend's introduction, hoping to work together to achieve the purpose of serving society and promoting industry. Unexpectedly, Mr. Wu Liang has become insane in the past two years, greedy for small profits, impersonating domestic factory trademarks, and indiscriminately selling Japanese goods. Recently, he has even intensified his efforts and used tricks to sabotage the national products movement. Ms. Zhang Yongzhen, based on her patriotic enthusiasm, has repeatedly advised him, but he insists on going his own way and does not care. Recently, due to incompatible ideas and deteriorating feelings, Ms. Zhang Yongzhen, for the sake of her personality, is unwilling to live with this person who recognizes a thief as a father. In addition to reporting Wu Liang's bad deeds of indiscriminately selling Japanese goods to the Women's National Products Movement Committee, she also announced the severance of her marriage relationship with Wu Liang, etc...."

×　　×　　×　　×

This is the Women's National Products Year. The wave of women promoting national products will inevitably give those who underestimate "women" an iron lesson.

Let the Women Handle It

— Xuan Wan

Last year [National Products Year], throughout the entire year, we were truly tired of shouting all the slogans for promoting national products, but what were the results? What was revealed to us was a trade deficit of 900 million yuan, setting a new record never seen before. Seeing the Eastern and Western foreign devils laughing heartily, reflected that our national products industry was shouting itself hoarse, with no one responding. If we think carefully about this responsibility, of course, our national women's community cannot escape it. Therefore, starting this year, it is designated as the Women's National Products Year [Let the Women Handle It], with our national female compatriots jointly taking responsibility to promote and use national products. Naturally, this great driving force will be much more practical than last year's empty words and high-sounding theories. However, judging from the current situation, we should absolutely observe both aspects at the same time, which is the difference between urban women and rural women in their attitude towards national product issues, which needs to be analyzed and studied by us.

(1) Urban Women. The dumping of most foreign goods is aimed at urban women as their direct consumers. The so-called modern women, from head to toe, all take pride in wearing foreign goods. Cosmetics, silks, and all household daily necessities, which one is not purchased by their delicate jade hands, with money flowing out in torrents. How can we not be surprised and amazed by this painful fact? But upon closer examination, the reason why urban women are like this is only because they are misled by a hateful vanity and bound by the general bad habits of society, so the loss of their nature is only temporary.

(2) Rural Women. Our country was originally an agricultural country, with its own mulberry farming and weaving, and the handicraft industry was very prosperous. Therefore, initially, there was no need for imported goods at all. However, since the opening of the sea, foreign goods have been dumped like mercury leaking onto the ground, and there has been no hole that they have not penetrated. Of course, rural women also purchase foreign goods, such as foreign cloth, matches, and all daily necessities, due to mixing fish eyes with pearls or because of the lure of low prices.

Then, based on the above facts, we can get a clear view. In relation to urban women and rural women, regarding the rejection of national products and the enjoyment of foreign goods, they have a clear distinction. One is entirely due to the instigation of vanity, and the other is due to the lure of low prices or simply blind purchasing. Therefore, our future work will be to guide them separately in this way in order to achieve complete success.

Family Visit Record

Mrs. Yang Weiyu

— Tianyun

Mrs. Yang Weiyu, is also Ms. Peng Wangfen, who is known for her literature. Ms. Peng graduated from teacher training and is a genius in literature. She works as a Chinese teacher at the China Vocational School. Her most proud work is a book published by the China Vocational Education Society called [Min'er's Mother], which is written with deep emotion and is deeply admired by readers. Recently, Mr. Yang and Ms. Peng participated in the Women's National Products Year Movement and wrote several articles for various newspapers promoting national products, which shows their enthusiasm and perseverance. One day, a reporter specially visited the home of Mr. and Mrs. Yang. The small room was very clean and simple. The tables, chairs, boxes, and cabinets were all arranged neatly. Mr. Yang was wearing cloth clothes, and Mrs. Yang was wearing domestic silks. Recently, Mr. Yang had a new set of domestic wool student clothes made, and Mrs. Yang also had a domestic wool coat made. The three children were all lively and wore domestic clothes, jumping back from school. Mrs. Yang also returned home after class to fulfill her duties as a mother. Mr. Yang came from a poor family. Recently, he published his [The Night Before Leaving Home] in [The Great Wall] , which was written with deep sincerity. Therefore, his daily life can be said to be simple and content. Mrs. Yang came from a prominent family in Wumen and was accustomed to being pampered since childhood, but after coming to the Yang family, she abandoned makeup, avoided extravagance, and was also diligent and thrifty, living the life of Liang Meng. They also implemented a policy of budgeting and final accounting when spending money. Currently, almost everything they wear, eat, and use is exclusively domestic products. Every needle, every thread, and every match is only sought from domestic products. Once, Mrs. Yang said to me, "I have traveled all over the China National Products Company and could not buy a single domestic needle. Later, after my investigation, the China National Products Company recently had products from the Qingdao Needle Company." Mrs. Yang said, "[During the Women's National Products Year, promoting national products can only start from household items. Domestic products have been improving day by day in recent years. In terms of clothing, food, and housing, whatever foreign products have, domestic products have as well. The decoration is beautiful and not inferior to foreign products, and they are economical and durable, and even surpass them. Why must we learn foreign airs and depend on foreign goods? For example, China has many fine candies, why must we have [chocolate]? Europeans and Americans all praise Huadiao wine, why must we have [whiskey]? China has many new products of silks, cloths, and wools, why must we have [Vienna], [Flannel], [Paris Satin]? Therefore, from now on, as long as we women first eliminate foreign goods and promote domestic goods within the scope of our households, this year's achievements will definitely be considerable. I hope that many women's groups will all get up and do it. I think the most easily visible thing this year is that the alarming number of imported goods can definitely be reduced." Ms. Peng's insights, and her enthusiasm and perseverance in implementing the promotion of national products, are truly admirable. Ms. Peng's family's simple and simple use of domestic products is especially worthy of our visit.

Contributions from the Women's Community

Rational Concepts

— Nie Zeng Jifen

Today, in discussing methods for promoting national products, please separate them from resisting foreign goods and enemy goods, and from promoting national products, and seek their prerequisite issues; First, we should promote rational concepts among Chinese people. Today, all kinds of failures in our country, and the corruption of various countries in the world, are all due to erroneous concepts. The main point is that pride in luxury and wealth is considered valuable, while being humble, poor, and lowly is considered shameful. Today, people often talk about promoting desires to promote culture, but in fact, desires and culture do not stand side by side. Only Eastern philosophers respect experience, and their theories are contrary to this, rewarding poverty and frugality, and condemning luxury and wealth. As for encouraging diligence and condemning pride and laziness, it goes without saying. Not to mention the times before the Zhou Dynasty, since the Han Dynasty, famous politicians, and poets since the Jin Dynasty, have had this clear expression, and those who established it as a theory were Confucius and Mencius. In the Analects, there are more than a dozen places where wealth and honor are condemned and poverty and frugality are rewarded. For example, Yan Hui's contentment with a bamboo basket of rice and a gourd of water in a humble alley, and Zilu's lack of shame in wearing a tattered robe, are all praised for their virtue. Yu the Great's meager diet, humble palaces, and distaste for fine clothes are all praised in admiration. All human beings inherently have the inferior roots of valuing wealth and despising poverty, and even with strong correction, it is difficult to change. Moreover, today, the evil wind of Western worship of money is being imported. What was considered wrong in the past is now considered right. Wherever there is profit, nothing is impossible, thus creating this deformed society and critical situation. The outflow of money, the withering of industry, and the large number of unemployed are all due to this.

In recent years, the surge in the import of foreign goods has been shocking. There are many reasons, but the advancement of fashion and art is a major aspect. In the past, female factory workers all wore short jackets made of coarse blue cloth. In recent years, most of them have cut their hair and wear long robes made of printed fine cloth. This clothing is beautiful and very cheap. The material for a robe costs only about two yuan. Female workers earn more than ten yuan a month, and they believe that they can afford it, so they are not stingy. However, each person needs to prepare three pieces for winter, summer, and spring. It is known without asking what country this cheap and beautiful printed fine cloth comes from. Families with better occupations make more beautiful clothes. In Shanghai alone, there are tens of thousands of female workers, and millions of other women. Extrapolating to the whole country, it accumulates into an astonishingly large number. For more than ten years, students have been competing to wear Western suits, which has already been a large expenditure, and the supplies associated with Western suits are even more enormous. Wealthy people's shoes and socks cost dozens of yuan, and they must change their clothes every time they go out, with those in high positions and those with higher education taking the lead in promoting it, and newspapers and newspapers promoting and encouraging it, and the whole country is swept away by it. Now, to remedy it, we still need to start with social leaders and women as role models, with simple decorations that are appropriate, so that everyone can create a new concept, considering thrift and simplicity as reasonable and splendor as unreasonable, and then we can talk about promoting national products. Gandhi advocated wearing cloth made of hand-spun yarn, using coarse cloth as a symbol of patriotism, and British exports to England dropped by half, which is ironclad evidence.

I have more to say, that is, recently women have been imitating Westerners by exposing their arms and legs, wearing high heels and long silk stockings, which is very meaningless. Nations should each have an independent spirit, how can they chase after others. Moreover, this kind of dress is not hygienic. I have seen friends who have broken their leg bones because of high heels, and it usually hinders operations, not to mention it. In winter, many people have colds and cannot leave their noses without handkerchiefs. Is it wise to sacrifice health and even life to pursue fashion? Curling hair into a curly shape, and having to go to a hair salon to do it, costs money and time, which is unnecessary. These are all unconscious behaviors of Westerners, and it is especially important to know that they are not things that should be in a reasonable life. What I have seen of Japanese women is that for fifty years, their clothing has not changed slightly, and except for prostitutes, almost no one has cut their hair. Can what our people do avoid their sneers?

Women's Talk on National Products

Grandma's Tips on Everyday Life

— Yu Qiacheng

亅Economic Recovery of Lost Territory丨

If you don't understand what the National Goods Movement is, or doubt the Women's National Goods Year, what I'm about to tell you isn't just empty talk, but a reminder of an old saying. It's said that since the opening of China to foreign trade, foreigners have given us three great gifts, or magic weapons: cannons, the Bible, and foreign goods.

Under the magic of cannons, from the Opium War to the January 28th Incident and the September 18th Incident, the benefits we've received, from the cession of Hong Kong to the Luan River war zone, have been the loss of all our vassal states and the change in color of our map. To this day, we are still calling for the recovery of lost territory.

The Bible issue seems to have shifted now. Christianity has mostly been transferred from foreign missionaries to Chinese believers. The past is gone, but the future is still within reach, so let's leave that aside for now.

Foreign goods were originally rare and exotic items, but the annual outflow of hundreds of millions of dollars is given to others because we consume foreign goods. This not only leads to our own people's poverty and depletion of wealth, but also makes many foreigners who come to China to sell goods rich. It is said that the guns and bullets they use to fight us contain the blood and sweat that they have squeezed from us.

This is the most reasonable calculation. If a family that is becoming increasingly poor and defeated wants to seek prosperity, the only way to do so is to start with thrift. This is what is meant by increasing income and reducing expenditure. Applying this principle to our economically distressed country, the only way to do it is to protect our original vitality and not let it be depleted. In other words, stop buying foreign goods and don't let money flow out of the country.

However, to go a step further, our daily lives cannot be forever self-sufficient, and we will inevitably have to buy things from outside. Therefore, we should understand that after curing a disease by removing the toxins, we must also cultivate our own original vitality. Then, we should cherish and promote domestically produced goods, because this is our own foundation, and only in this way can we achieve the goal of economic recovery of lost territory!

Accordingly, at the beginning of this Women's National Goods Year, when the women are responsible for doing the work, we must first establish these two concepts…

Why do we want to promote national goods? To achieve economic recovery of lost territory!

Why do we want to consume national goods? To achieve economic recovery of lost territory!

Cosmetics

— Hanyu

Setting: A richly decorated drawing room.

Time: 5 PM on a certain afternoon.

Characters: Father, Mother, Daughter.

(The curtain rises, the father is smoking in the drawing room, the daughter comes out from inside.)

Daughter: Dad... I want to go out and buy some things!

Father: What do you want to buy? (Puts hand into pocket, as if to take out money.)

Daughter: I want to buy some cosmetics.

Father: (Looking surprised.) Cosmetics? Isn't it better to use the ones we make ourselves? (Takes hand out of pocket.)

Daughter: The ones we make ourselves are only fit for workers to use. How could we possibly use them? (Acts haughty.)

Father: (Slightly angry.) You don't use the ones we make ourselves, but you want to use foreign goods. Do you know what patriotism is?

Daughter: (Turns her back to her father.) Patriotism is just a slogan. Anyway, I want to buy French goods.

Father: (Angry.) Patriotism is a slogan? Is that what you should be saying? I opened a cosmetics factory for the sake of patriotism. Is that also just a slogan? You want to abandon national goods and use foreign goods. That's the mentality of a slave!

Daughter: Don't you know? All my classmates use foreign goods. If I'm the only one using national goods, won't they laugh at me?

Father: (Very angry.) People will laugh at you for using national goods? They're willing to be slaves of a fallen nation. Are you also willing to be a slave of a fallen nation? The country has become so bad. It's all your fault! Now that the Women's National Goods Year is almost here, you still want to use foreign goods? Can you be considered a woman? Can you be considered a human being? Your classmates use foreign goods, you should persuade them to use national goods. It is the responsibility of every citizen to promote national goods. When I was in Japan, I saw that none of their people used foreign goods. That's a very good example! China is going to be ruined because everyone wants to use foreign goods! (Slams the table.)

Mother: (Coming out from inside.) What are you arguing about?

Father: (Pointing at the daughter to the mother.) We have our own cosmetics but she won't use them. She still wants to use foreign goods.

Mother: (To the daughter.) Why do you still want to use foreign goods? The ones we make ourselves are almost the same as foreign goods.

Daughter: I just don't believe that national goods are almost the same as foreign goods.

Mother: Isn't what I put on my face made by us? (Points to her face.)

Daughter: (Gets close to the mother, sniffs slightly.) This is produced by ×× Company. You're still trying to deceive me by saying it's national goods.

Mother: You don't believe me? Isn't what's on my dressing table made by us?

Daughter: You're trying to deceive me?

Mother: Why would I deceive you?

Daughter: Then I'll use national goods.

(Curtain closes.)

The National Goods Scripture

— Xu Nangong

In the National Goods Year, using national goods is as right as rain, unshakeable. Chinese people using Chinese goods, the nation prospers and wealth abounds. Factories rush to produce national goods, quality is excellent and sales are widespread. Crude and shoddy manufacturing is the wrong path, the survival of the fittest is inevitable. Stores sell domestically produced goods, business is booming and there are many customers. Don't try to disguise foreign goods as domestic, running dogs of merchants will eventually fail. Elderly people using domestic goods, live long, healthy, and wealthy lives. If you buy and use foreign goods, people will see you as senile. Wives should use Chinese goods, more happiness, longer lives, and great fortune. If you buy and use foreign goods, iron birds and bombs will bring disaster. Grandmothers who use Chinese goods are called virtuous mothers and good wives. If you use foreign goods, people will laugh and scold you as old spinsters. Young ladies should use domestic goods, modern and beautiful, that's the fashionable way. Anyone who buys and uses foreign goods will have a hard time marrying a good husband. Young people should use Chinese goods, single-mindedly save the country, don't be frivolous. If you love to use foreign goods, you will inevitably become a slave of a fallen nation. All Chinese people should use national goods, protect the country, protect the home, and protect the mountains and rivers. National goods are manufactured better than foreign goods, cheap, good quality, and many colors. Please don't think I'm blowing my own trumpet, economic invasion is as harmful as a tiger. The corner of the Northeast is broken, everyone must remember clearly. Everyone should rush to use national goods, the prison of a fallen nation can still be repaired.
